STRAP-ViT: Segregated Tokens with Randomized -- Transformations for Defense against Adversarial Patches in ViTs
Authors: Nandish Chattopadhyay, Anadi Goyal, Chandan Karfa, Anupam Chattopadhyay
First: 2026-03-13T06:03:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T06:03:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication at IEEE/ACM Design Automation Conference (DAC) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Adversarial patches are physically realizable localized noise, which are able to hijack Vision Transformers (ViT) self-attention, pulling focus toward a small, high-contrast region and corrupting the class token to force confident misclassifications. In this paper, we claim that the tokens which correspond to the areas of the image that contain the adversarial noise, have different statistical properties when compared to the tokens which do not overlap with the adversarial perturbations. We use this insight to propose a mechanism, called STRAP-ViT, which uses Jensen-Shannon Divergence as a metric for segregating tokens that behave as anomalies in the Detection Phase, and then apply randomized composite transformations on them during the Mitigation Phase to make the adversarial noise ineffective. The minimum number of tokens to transform is a hyper-parameter for the defense mechanism and is chosen such that at least 50% of the patch is covered by the transformed tokens. STRAP-ViT fits as a non-trainable plug-and-play block within the ViT architectures, for inference purposes only, with a minimal computational cost and does not require any additional training cost/effort. STRAP-ViT has been tested on multiple pre-trained vision transformer architectures (ViT-base-16 and DinoV2) and datasets (ImageNet and CalTech-101), across multiple adversarial attacks (Adversarial Patch, LAVAN, GDPA and RP2), and found to provide excellent robust accuracies lying within a 2-3% range of the clean baselines, and outperform the state-of-the-art.

标题：STRAP-ViT：用于防御ViT中的对抗性补丁的随机化变换的分离令牌
对抗性补丁是可物理实现的局部噪声，能够劫持视觉变换器（ViT）的自注意力，将焦点拉向一个小的高对比度区域，并破坏类别令牌以强制产生自信的错误分类。本文声称，与不重叠对抗性扰动的令牌相比，包含对抗性噪声的图像区域对应的令牌具有不同的统计特性。我们利用这一见解提出了一种机制，称为STRAP-ViT，使用Jensen-Shannon散度作为度量，在检测阶段分离表现为异常的令牌，然后在缓解阶段对其应用随机复合变换，使对抗性噪声失效。需要变换的最小令牌数量是防御机制的超参数，选择时确保至少50%的补丁被变换后的令牌覆盖。STRAP-ViT作为一个不可训练的即插即用模块适用于ViT架构，仅用于推理，具有最小的计算成本，并且不需要额外的训练成本/努力。STRAP-ViT已在多个预训练的视觉变换器架构（ViT-base-16和DinoV2）和数据集（ImageNet和CalTech-101）上进行了测试，针对多种对抗性攻击（对抗性补丁、LAVAN、GDPA和RP2），发现其提供的鲁棒准确率在干净基线的2-3%范围内，且优于当前最先进的技术。

Follow the Saliency: Supervised Saliency for Retrieval-augmented Dense Video Captioning
Authors: Seung hee Choi, MinJu Jeon, Hyunwoo Oh, Jihwan Lee, Dong-Jin Kim
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-12T02:37:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T05:50:31+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026 accepted paper (main track)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Existing retrieval-augmented approaches for Dense Video Captioning (DVC) often fail to achieve accurate temporal segmentation aligned with true event boundaries, as they rely on heuristic strategies that overlook ground truth event boundaries. The proposed framework, \textbf{STaRC}, overcomes this limitation by supervising frame-level saliency through a highlight detection module. Note that the highlight detection module is trained on binary labels derived directly from DVC ground truth annotations without the need for additional annotation. We also propose to utilize the saliency scores as a unified temporal signal that drives retrieval via saliency-guided segmentation and informs caption generation through explicit Saliency Prompts injected into the decoder. By enforcing saliency-constrained segmentation, our method produces temporally coherent segments that align closely with actual event transitions, leading to more accurate retrieval and contextually grounded caption generation. We conduct comprehensive evaluations on the YouCook2 and ViTT benchmarks, where STaRC achieves state-of-the-art performance across most of the metrics. Our code is available at https://github.com/ermitaju1/STaRC

Why Neural Structural Obfuscation Can't Kill White-Box Watermarks for Good!
Authors: Yanna Jiang, Guangsheng Yu, Qingyuan Yu, Yi Chen, Qin Wang
First: 2026-03-13T05:50:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T05:50:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural Structural Obfuscation (NSO) (USENIX Security'23) is a family of ``zero cost'' structure-editing transforms (\texttt{nso\_zero}, \texttt{nso\_clique}, \texttt{nso\_split}) that inject dummy neurons. By combining neuron permutation and parameter scaling, NSO makes a radical modification to the network structure and parameters while strictly preserving functional equivalence, thereby disrupting white-box watermark verification. This capability has been a fundamental challenge to the reliability of existing white-box watermarking schemes. We rethink NSO and, for the first time, fully recover from the damage it has caused. We redefine NSO as a graph-consistent threat model within a \textit{producer--consumer} paradigm. This formulation posits that any obfuscation of a producer node necessitates a compatible layout update in all downstream consumers to maintain structural integrity. Building on these consistency constraints on signal propagation, we present \textsc{Canon}, a recovery framework that probes the attacked model to identify redundancy/dummy channels and then \textit{globally} canonicalizes the network by rewriting \textit{all} downstream consumers by construction, synchronizing layouts across \texttt{fan-out}, \texttt{add}, and \texttt{cat}. Extensive experiments demonstrate that, even under strong composed and extended NSO attacks, \textsc{Canon} achieves \textbf{100\%} recovery success, restoring watermark verifiability while preserving task utility. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/anti-NSO-9874.
中文标题/摘要
标题：为什么神经结构混淆无法彻底消除白盒水印！
神经结构混淆（NSO）（USENIX Security'23）是一类“零成本”结构编辑变换（\texttt{nso\_zero}，\texttt{nso\_clique}，\texttt{nso\_split}），通过注入虚拟神经元。通过结合神经元置换和参数缩放，NSO对网络结构和参数进行了根本性的修改，同时严格保持功能等价，从而干扰白盒水印验证。这一能力对现有白盒水印方案的可靠性构成了根本挑战。 我们重新思考NSO，并首次完全恢复其造成的损害。我们将NSO重新定义为一种在\textit{生产者-消费者}范式下的图一致性威胁模型。该公式假设，任何对生产者节点的混淆都需要在所有下游消费者中进行兼容的布局更新，以保持结构完整性。在这些信号传播的一致性约束基础上，我们提出了\textsc{Canon}，一个恢复框架，探测被攻击的模型以识别冗余/虚拟通道，然后通过构造全局规范化网络，重写\textit{所有}下游消费者，跨\texttt{fan-out}、\texttt{add}和\texttt{cat}同步布局。大量实验表明，即使在强大的复合和扩展NSO攻击下，\textsc{Canon}也能实现\textbf{100\%}的恢复成功，恢复水印可验证性，同时保持任务效用。 我们的代码可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/anti-NSO-9874获取。

The authors propose a recovery framework called Canon that redefines NSO within a producer-consumer paradigm, focusing on maintaining structural integrity through consistency constraints on signal propagation. Experimental results show that Canon achieves 100% recovery success in restoring watermark verifiability, even when subjected to strong NSO attacks, while also preserving the utility of the tasks performed by the neural networks.
本研究的动机在于解决神经结构混淆（NSO）对白盒水印方案可靠性带来的挑战。作者提出了一种名为Canon的恢复框架，将NSO重新定义为图一致性威胁模型，并利用信号传播的一致性约束来恢复混淆造成的损害。实验结果表明，Canon在遭受强NSO攻击时实现了100%的恢复成功率，恢复了水印的可验证性，同时保持了任务的有效性。
Uncovering Security Threats and Architecting Defenses in Autonomous Agents: A Case Study of OpenClaw
Authors: Zonghao Ying, Xiao Yang, Siyang Wu, Yumeng Song, Yang Qu, Hainan Li, Tianlin Li, Jiakai Wang, Aishan Liu, Xianglong Liu
First: 2026-03-13T04:33:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T04:33:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The rapid evolution of Large Language Models (LLMs) into autonomous, tool-calling agents has fundamentally altered the cybersecurity landscape. Frameworks like OpenClaw grant AI systems operating-system-level permissions and the autonomy to execute complex workflows. This level of access creates unprecedented security challenges. Consequently, traditional content-filtering defenses have become obsolete. This report presents a comprehensive security analysis of the OpenClaw ecosystem. We systematically investigate its current threat landscape, highlighting critical vulnerabilities such as prompt injection-driven Remote Code Execution (RCE), sequential tool attack chains, context amnesia, and supply chain contamination. To systematically contextualize these threats, we propose a novel tri-layered risk taxonomy for autonomous Agents, categorizing vulnerabilities across AI Cognitive, Software Execution, and Information System dimensions. To address these systemic architectural flaws, we introduce the Full-Lifecycle Agent Security Architecture (FASA). This theoretical defense blueprint advocates for zero-trust agentic execution, dynamic intent verification, and cross-layer reasoning-action correlation. Building on this framework, we present Project ClawGuard, our ongoing engineering initiative. This project aims to implement the FASA paradigm and transition autonomous agents from high-risk experimental utilities into trustworthy systems. Our code and dataset are available at https://github.com/NY1024/ClawGuard.

RTD-Guard: A Black-Box Textual Adversarial Detection Framework via Replacement Token Detection
Authors: He Zhu, Yanshu Li, Wen Liu, Haitian Yang
First: 2026-03-13T02:30:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T02:30:56+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Textual adversarial attacks pose a serious security threat to Natural Language Processing (NLP) systems by introducing imperceptible perturbations that mislead deep learning models. While adversarial example detection offers a lightweight alternative to robust training, existing methods typically rely on prior knowledge of attacks, white-box access to the victim model, or numerous queries, which severely limits their practical deployment. This paper introduces RTD-Guard, a novel black-box framework for detecting textual adversarial examples. Our key insight is that word-substitution perturbations in adversarial attacks closely resemble the "replaced tokens" that a Replaced Token Detection (RTD) discriminator is pre-trained to identify. Leveraging this, RTD-Guard employs an off-the-shelf RTD discriminator-without fine-tuning-to localize suspicious tokens, masks them, and detects adversarial examples by observing the prediction confidence shift of the victim model before and after intervention. The entire process requires no adversarial data, model tuning, or internal model access, and uses only two black-box queries. Comprehensive experiments on multiple benchmark datasets demonstrate that RTD-Guard effectively detects adversarial texts generated by diverse state-of-the-art attack methods. It surpasses existing detection baselines across multiple metrics, offering a highly efficient, practical, and resource-light defense mechanism-particularly suited for real-world deployment in resource-constrained or privacy-sensitive environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RTD-Guard：一种通过替换标记检测的黑箱文本对抗检测框架
文本对抗攻击通过引入不可察觉的扰动，对自然语言处理（NLP）系统构成严重的安全威胁，误导深度学习模型。虽然对抗样本检测提供了一种轻量级的替代方案，但现有方法通常依赖于对攻击的先验知识、对受害模型的白箱访问或大量查询，这严重限制了它们的实际部署。本文介绍了RTD-Guard，一种新颖的黑箱框架，用于检测文本对抗样本。我们的关键见解是，对抗攻击中的词替换扰动与替换标记检测（RTD）判别器预训练识别的“替换标记”非常相似。利用这一点，RTD-Guard采用现成的RTD判别器——无需微调——来定位可疑标记，屏蔽它们，并通过观察受害模型在干预前后的预测置信度变化来检测对抗样本。整个过程不需要对抗数据、模型调优或内部模型访问，仅使用两个黑箱查询。在多个基准数据集上的全面实验表明，RTD-Guard有效检测由多种最先进攻击方法生成的对抗文本。它在多个指标上超越了现有检测基线，提供了一种高效、实用且资源轻量的防御机制，特别适合在资源受限或隐私敏感的环境中进行实际部署。

Agent Privilege Separation in OpenClaw: A Structural Defense Against Prompt Injection
Authors: Darren Cheng, Wen-Kwang Tsao
First: 2026-03-13T02:03:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T02:03:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Prompt injection remains one of the most practical attack vectors against LLM-integrated applications. We replicate the Microsoft LLMail-Inject benchmark (Greshake et al., 2024) against current generation models running inside OpenClaw, an open source multitool agent platform. Our proposed defense combines two mechanisms: agent isolation, implemented as a privilege separated two-agent pipeline with tool partitioning, and JSON formatting, which produces structured output that strips persuasive framing before the action agent processes it. We run four experiments on the same 649 attacks that succeeded against our single-agent baseline. The full pipeline achieves 0 percent attack success rate (ASR) on the evaluated benchmark. Agent isolation alone achieves 0.31 percent ASR, approximately 323 times lower than the baseline. JSON formatting alone achieves 14.18 percent ASR, about 7.1 times lower. Our ablation study confirms that agent isolation is the dominant mechanism. JSON formatting provides additional hardening but is not sufficient on its own. The defense is structural: the action agent never receives raw injection content regardless of model behavior on any individual input.

Lyapunov Stable Graph Neural Flow
Authors: Haoyu Chu, Xiaotong Chen, Wei Zhou, Wenjun Cui, Kai Zhao, Shikui Wei, Qiyu Kang
First: 2026-03-13T01:40:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T01:40:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) are highly vulnerable to adversarial perturbations in both topology and features, making the learning of robust representations a critical challenge. In this work, we bridge GNNs with control theory to introduce a novel defense framework grounded in integer- and fractional-order Lyapunov stability. Unlike conventional strategies that rely on resource-heavy adversarial training or data purification, our approach fundamentally constrains the underlying feature-update dynamics of the GNN. We propose an adaptive, learnable Lyapunov function paired with a novel projection mechanism that maps the network's state into a stable space, thereby offering theoretically provable stability guarantees. Notably, this mechanism is orthogonal to existing defenses, allowing for seamless integration with techniques like adversarial training to achieve cumulative robustness. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our Lyapunov-stable graph neural flows substantially outperform base neural flows and state-of-the-art baselines across standard benchmarks and various adversarial attack scenarios.

Partially Recentralization Softmax Loss for Vision-Language Models Robustness
Authors: Hao Wang, Jinzhe Jiang, Xin Zhang, Chen Li
First: 2024-02-06T01:44:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T01:07:31+00:00
Comments: The study described in Section 4 was conducted without required institutional review board approval. The paper is withdrawn pending completion of the approval process
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As Large Language Models make a breakthrough in natural language processing tasks (NLP), multimodal technique becomes extremely popular. However, it has been shown that multimodal NLP are vulnerable to adversarial attacks, where the outputs of a model can be dramatically changed by a perturbation to the input. While several defense techniques have been proposed both in computer vision and NLP models, the multimodal robustness of models have not been fully explored. In this paper, we study the adversarial robustness provided by modifying loss function of pre-trained multimodal models, by restricting top K softmax outputs. Based on the evaluation and scoring, our experiments show that after a fine-tuning, adversarial robustness of pre-trained models can be significantly improved, against popular attacks. Further research should be studying, such as output diversity, generalization and the robustness-performance trade-off of this kind of loss functions. Our code will be available after this paper is accepted

Generalization and Memorization in Rectified Flow
Authors: Mingxing Rao, Daniel Moyer
First: 2026-03-12T21:10:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T21:10:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative models based on the Flow Matching objective, particularly Rectified Flow, have emerged as a dominant paradigm for efficient, high-fidelity image synthesis. However, while existing research heavily prioritizes generation quality and architectural scaling, the underlying dynamics of how RF models memorize training data remain largely underexplored. In this paper, we systematically investigate the memorization behaviors of RF through the test statistics of Membership Inference Attacks (MIA). We progressively formulate three test statistics, culminating in a complexity-calibrated metric ($T_\text{mc\_cal}$) that successfully decouples intrinsic image spatial complexity from genuine memorization signals. This calibration yields a significant performance surge -- boosting attack AUC by up to 15\% and the privacy-critical TPR@1\%FPR metric by up to 45\% -- establishing the first non-trivial MIA specifically tailored for RF. Leveraging these refined metrics, we uncover a distinct temporal pattern: under standard uniform temporal training, a model's susceptibility to MIA strictly peaks at the integration midpoint, a phenomenon we justify via the network's forced deviation from linear approximations. Finally, we demonstrate that substituting uniform timestep sampling with a Symmetric Exponential (U-shaped) distribution effectively minimizes exposure to vulnerable intermediate timesteps. Extensive evaluations across three datasets confirm that this temporal regularization suppresses memorization while preserving generative fidelity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：修正流中的泛化与记忆
基于流匹配目标的生成模型，特别是修正流，已成为高效、高保真图像合成的主导范式。然而，尽管现有研究高度重视生成质量和架构扩展，但修正流模型如何记忆训练数据的基本动态仍然未被充分探索。本文系统地通过成员推断攻击（MIA）的测试统计量研究修正流的记忆行为。我们逐步制定了三个测试统计量，最终形成了一个复杂度校准指标（$T_\text{mc\_cal}$），成功地将内在图像空间复杂性与真实记忆信号解耦。这种校准带来了显著的性能提升——攻击AUC提高了多达15\%，隐私关键的TPR@1\%FPR指标提高了多达45\%——建立了第一个专门针对修正流的非平凡MIA。利用这些精细化指标，我们发现了一种独特的时间模式：在标准均匀时间训练下，模型对MIA的敏感性在积分中点严格达到峰值，这一现象通过网络强制偏离线性近似得以解释。最后，我们证明用对称指数（U形）分布替代均匀时间步采样有效地最小化了对脆弱中间时间步的暴露。对三个数据集的广泛评估确认，这种时间正则化抑制了记忆，同时保持了生成的保真度。

Additionally, they demonstrate that using a U-shaped distribution for timestep sampling can effectively reduce memorization without compromising generative quality.

Accelerating Suffix Jailbreak attacks with Prefix-Shared KV-cache
Authors: Xinhai Wang, Shaopeng Fu, Shu Yang, Liangyu Wang, Tianhang Zheng, Di Wang
First: 2026-03-12T21:07:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T21:07:20+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 3 figures, preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Suffix jailbreak attacks serve as a systematic method for red-teaming Large Language Models (LLMs) but suffer from prohibitive computational costs, as a large number of candidate suffixes need to be evaluated before identifying a jailbreak suffix. This paper presents Prefix-Shared KV Cache (PSKV), a plug-and-play inference optimization technique tailored for jailbreak suffix generation. Our method is motivated by a key observation that when performing suffix jailbreaking, while a large number of candidate prompts need to be evaluated, they share the same targeted harmful instruction as the prefix. Therefore, instead of performing redundant inference on the duplicated prefix, PSKV maintains a single KV cache for this prefix and shares it with every candidate prompt, enabling the parallel inference of diverse suffixes with minimal memory overhead. This design enables more aggressive batching strategies that would otherwise be limited by memory constraints. Extensive experiments on six widely used suffix attacks across five widely deployed LLMs demonstrate that PSKV reduces inference time by 40\% and peak memory usage by 50\%, while maintaining the original Attack Success Rate (ASR). The code has been submitted and will be released publicly.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过前缀共享KV缓存加速后缀越狱攻击
后缀越狱攻击作为一种系统化的方法用于对大型语言模型（LLMs）进行红队测试，但由于需要评估大量候选后缀，导致计算成本高昂。本文提出了前缀共享KV缓存（PSKV），这是一种针对越狱后缀生成的即插即用推理优化技术。我们的方法基于一个关键观察：在进行后缀越狱时，虽然需要评估大量候选提示，但它们与前缀共享相同的目标有害指令。因此，PSKV维护一个针对该前缀的单一KV缓存，并与每个候选提示共享，从而实现多样后缀的并行推理，内存开销最小化。这一设计使得更激进的批处理策略成为可能，而不会受到内存限制的影响。在五个广泛部署的LLM上对六种广泛使用的后缀攻击进行的广泛实验表明，PSKV将推理时间减少了40\%，峰值内存使用减少了50\%，同时保持了原始攻击成功率（ASR）。代码已提交并将公开发布。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the high computational costs associated with suffix jailbreak attacks on Large Language Models (LLMs), which require evaluating numerous candidate suffixes. The authors propose a new inference optimization technique called Prefix-Shared KV Cache (PSKV), which leverages the observation that many candidate prompts share the same harmful instruction as their prefix, allowing for a single KV cache to be used across multiple prompts. Experimental results show that PSKV significantly reduces inference time by 40% and peak memory usage by 50% while maintaining the original Attack Success Rate (ASR) across six suffix attacks tested on five different LLMs.

SpectralGuard: Detecting Memory Collapse Attacks in State Space Models
Authors: Davi Bonetto
First: 2026-03-12T19:52:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T19:52:37+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 10 figures. Code, dataset, and demo: https://github.com/DaviBonetto/spectralguard
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
State Space Models (SSMs) such as Mamba achieve linear-time sequence processing through input-dependent recurrence, but this mechanism introduces a critical safety vulnerability. We show that the spectral radius rho(A-bar) of the discretized transition operator governs effective memory horizon: when an adversary drives rho toward zero through gradient-based Hidden State Poisoning, memory collapses from millions of tokens to mere dozens, silently destroying reasoning capacity without triggering output-level alarms. We prove an Evasion Existence Theorem showing that for any output-only defense, adversarial inputs exist that simultaneously induce spectral collapse and evade detection, then introduce SpectralGuard, a real-time monitor that tracks spectral stability across all model layers. SpectralGuard achieves F1=0.961 against non-adaptive attackers and retains F1=0.842 under the strongest adaptive setting, with sub-15ms per-token latency. Causal interventions and cross-architecture transfer to hybrid SSM-Attention systems confirm that spectral monitoring provides a principled, deployable safety layer for recurrent foundation models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SpectralGuard：在状态空间模型中检测内存崩溃攻击
状态空间模型（SSMs）如Mamba通过依赖输入的递归实现线性时间序列处理，但这一机制引入了关键的安全漏洞。我们表明，离散化转移算子的谱半径rho(A-bar)支配有效的记忆视野：当对手通过基于梯度的隐状态中毒将rho驱动至零时，记忆从数百万个标记崩溃至仅几十个，悄然破坏推理能力而不触发输出级警报。我们证明了一个规避存在定理，表明对于任何仅输出的防御，存在同时引发谱崩溃和规避检测的对抗输入，然后引入SpectralGuard，一个实时监控器，跟踪所有模型层的谱稳定性。SpectralGuard在非自适应攻击者下实现F1=0.961，在最强自适应设置下保持F1=0.842，每个标记延迟低于15毫秒。因果干预和跨架构转移到混合SSM-注意力系统确认谱监控为递归基础模型提供了一个原则性、可部署的安全层。

Security Considerations for Artificial Intelligence Agents
Authors: Ninghui Li, Kaiyuan Zhang, Kyle Polley, Jerry Ma
First: 2026-03-12T17:49:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T17:49:39+00:00
Comments: Perplexity Response to NIST/CAISI Request for Information 2025-0035. 91 Fed. Reg. 698 (Jan. 8, 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This article, a lightly adapted version of Perplexity's response to NIST/CAISI Request for Information 2025-0035, details our observations and recommendations concerning the security of frontier AI agents. These insights are informed by Perplexity's experience operating general-purpose agentic systems used by millions of users and thousands of enterprises in both controlled and open-world environments. Agent architectures change core assumptions around code-data separation, authority boundaries, and execution predictability, creating new confidentiality, integrity, and availability failure modes. We map principal attack surfaces across tools, connectors, hosting boundaries, and multi-agent coordination, with particular emphasis on indirect prompt injection, confused-deputy behavior, and cascading failures in long-running workflows. We then assess current defenses as a layered stack: input-level and model-level mitigations, sandboxed execution, and deterministic policy enforcement for high-consequence actions. Finally, we identify standards and research gaps, including adaptive security benchmarks, policy models for delegation and privilege control, and guidance for secure multi-agent system design aligned with NIST risk management principles.

CLASP: Defending Hybrid Large Language Models Against Hidden State Poisoning Attacks
Authors: Alexandre Le Mercier, Thomas Demeester, Chris Develder
First: 2026-03-12T17:29:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T17:29:55+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State space models (SSMs) like Mamba have gained significant traction as efficient alternatives to Transformers, achieving linear complexity while maintaining competitive performance. However, Hidden State Poisoning Attacks (HiSPAs), a recently discovered vulnerability that corrupts SSM memory through adversarial strings, pose a critical threat to these architectures and their hybrid variants. Framing the HiSPA mitigation task as a binary classification problem at the token level, we introduce the CLASP model to defend against this threat. CLASP exploits distinct patterns in Mamba's block output embeddings (BOEs) and uses an XGBoost classifier to identify malicious tokens with minimal computational overhead. We consider a realistic scenario in which both SSMs and HiSPAs are likely to be used: an LLM screening résumés to identify the best candidates for a role. Evaluated on a corpus of 2,483 résumés totaling 9.5M tokens with controlled injections, CLASP achieves 95.9% token-level F1 score and 99.3% document-level F1 score on malicious tokens detection. Crucially, the model generalizes to unseen attack patterns: under leave-one-out cross-validation, performance remains high (96.9% document-level F1), while under clustered cross-validation with structurally novel triggers, it maintains useful detection capability (91.6% average document-level F1). Operating independently of any downstream model, CLASP processes 1,032 tokens per second with under 4GB VRAM consumption, potentially making it suitable for real-world deployment as a lightweight front-line defense for SSM-based and hybrid architectures. All code and detailed results are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/hispikes-91C0.

状态空间模型（SSMs）如Mamba作为高效的Transformer替代方案获得了显著关注，达到了线性复杂度，同时保持了竞争力的性能。然而，隐藏状态中毒攻击（HiSPAs）是一种最近发现的漏洞，通过对抗字符串破坏SSM内存，对这些架构及其混合变体构成了严重威胁。将HiSPA缓解任务框架化为令牌级的二元分类问题，我们引入了CLASP模型以防御这一威胁。CLASP利用Mamba的块输出嵌入（BOEs）中的独特模式，并使用XGBoost分类器以最小的计算开销识别恶意令牌。我们考虑了一个现实场景，其中SSMs和HiSPAs可能同时使用：一个LLM筛选简历以识别最佳候选人。经过对2483份简历（总计9.5M令牌）进行控制注入的评估，CLASP在恶意令牌检测上达到了95.9%的令牌级F1分数和99.3%的文档级F1分数。重要的是，该模型对未见攻击模式具有良好的泛化能力：在留一交叉验证下，性能保持高水平（96.9%文档级F1），而在具有结构新颖触发器的聚类交叉验证下，仍保持有用的检测能力（91.6%平均文档级F1）。CLASP独立于任何下游模型，处理速度为每秒1032个令牌，VRAM消耗低于4GB，可能使其适合作为SSM基础和混合架构的轻量级前线防御进行实际部署。所有代码和详细结果可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/hispikes-91C0获取。

Understanding Disclosure Risk in Differential Privacy with Applications to Noise Calibration and Auditing (Extended Version)
Authors: Patricia Guerra-Balboa, Annika Sauer, Héber H. Arcolezi, Thorsten Strufe
First: 2026-03-12T16:43:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:43:55+00:00
Comments: This is an extended version of the paper accepted in the Proceedings of the VLDB Endowment (PVLDB), 2026. The code used for our experiments is accessible in https://github.com/PatriciaBalboaKIT/Understanding-Risk-in-DP
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Differential Privacy (DP) is widely adopted in data management systems to enable data sharing with formal disclosure guarantees. A central systems challenge is understanding how DP noise translates into effective protection against inference attacks, since this directly determines achievable utility. Most existing analyses focus only on membership inference -- capturing only a threat -- or rely on reconstruction robustness (ReRo). However, under realistic assumptions, we show that ReRo can yield misleading risk estimates and violate claimed bounds, limiting their usefulness for principled DP calibration and auditing. This paper introduces reconstruction advantage, a unified risk metric that consistently captures risk across membership inference, attribute inference, and data reconstruction. We derive tight bounds that relate DP noise to adversarial advantage and characterize optimal adversarial strategies for arbitrary DP mechanisms and attacker knowledge. These results enable risk-driven noise calibration and provide a foundation for systematic DP auditing. We show that reconstruction advantage improves the accuracy and scope of DP auditing and enables more effective utility-privacy trade-offs in DP-enabled data management systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：理解差分隐私中的披露风险及其在噪声校准和审计中的应用（扩展版）
差分隐私（DP）在数据管理系统中被广泛采用，以实现具有正式披露保证的数据共享。一个核心系统挑战是理解DP噪声如何转化为对推断攻击的有效保护，因为这直接决定了可实现的效用。现有的大多数分析仅关注成员推断——仅捕捉一种威胁——或依赖重建鲁棒性（ReRo）。然而，在现实假设下，我们表明ReRo可能导致误导性的风险估计并违反声称的界限，限制了其在原则性DP校准和审计中的实用性。本文引入重建优势，这是一种统一的风险度量，能够一致地捕捉成员推断、属性推断和数据重建的风险。我们推导出紧密的界限，将DP噪声与对抗优势相关联，并表征任意DP机制和攻击者知识的最佳对抗策略。这些结果使得基于风险的噪声校准成为可能，并为系统化的DP审计提供了基础。我们表明重建优势提高了DP审计的准确性和范围，并在DP支持的数据管理系统中实现了更有效的效用-隐私权衡。

EmbTracker: Traceable Black-box Watermarking for Federated Language Models
Authors: Haodong Zhao, Jinming Hu, Yijie Bai, Tian Dong, Wei Du, Zhuosheng Zhang, Yanjiao Chen, Haojin Zhu, Gongshen Liu
First: 2026-03-12T15:57:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T15:57:32+00:00
Comments: Work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Federated Language Model (FedLM) allows a collaborative learning without sharing raw data, yet it introduces a critical vulnerability, as every untrustworthy client may leak the received functional model instance. Current watermarking schemes for FedLM often require white-box access and client-side cooperation, providing only group-level proof of ownership rather than individual traceability. We propose EmbTracker, a server-side, traceable black-box watermarking framework specifically designed for FedLMs. EmbTracker achieves black-box verifiability by embedding a backdoor-based watermark detectable through simple API queries. Client-level traceability is realized by injecting unique identity-specific watermarks into the model distributed to each client. In this way, a leaked model can be attributed to a specific culprit, ensuring robustness even against non-cooperative participants. Extensive experiments on various language and vision-language models demonstrate that EmbTracker achieves robust traceability with verification rates near 100\%, high resilience against removal attacks (fine-tuning, pruning, quantization), and negligible impact on primary task performance (typically within 1-2\%).
中文标题/摘要
标题：EmbTracker：可追踪的黑箱水印技术用于联邦语言模型
联邦语言模型（FedLM）允许在不共享原始数据的情况下进行协作学习，但它引入了一个关键漏洞，因为每个不可信的客户端可能会泄露接收到的功能模型实例。目前针对FedLM的水印方案通常需要白箱访问和客户端合作，仅提供群体级的所有权证明，而不是个体可追溯性。我们提出了EmbTracker，这是一个专门为FedLM设计的服务器端可追踪黑箱水印框架。EmbTracker通过嵌入可通过简单API查询检测的基于后门的水印，实现黑箱可验证性。通过向分发给每个客户端的模型注入独特的身份特定水印，实现客户端级的可追溯性。通过这种方式，泄露的模型可以归因于特定的罪魁祸首，即使面对不合作的参与者也能确保鲁棒性。在各种语言和视觉语言模型上的广泛实验表明，EmbTracker实现了接近100%的验证率的鲁棒可追溯性，对去除攻击（微调、剪枝、量化）具有很高的抗性，并且对主要任务性能的影响微乎其微（通常在1-2%以内）。

本研究的动机在于解决联邦语言模型（FedLM）在不可信客户端可能泄露的脆弱性，因为现有的水印方法缺乏个体可追溯性并且需要客户端合作。作者提出了EmbTracker，这是一种服务器端的黑箱水印框架，通过将独特的身份特定水印嵌入分发给客户端的模型中，实现客户端级别的可追溯性，并通过简单的API查询实现黑箱可验证性。实验结果表明，EmbTracker的验证率接近100%，对各种去除攻击表现出较高的韧性，并且对主要任务性能的影响仅为1-2%。
Cascade: Composing Software-Hardware Attack Gadgets for Adversarial Threat Amplification in Compound AI Systems
Authors: Sarbartha Banerjee, Prateek Sahu, Anjo Vahldiek-Oberwagner, Jose Sanchez Vicarte, Mohit Tiwari
First: 2026-03-12T15:03:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T15:03:51+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 8 figures, 1 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rapid progress in generative AI has given rise to Compound AI systems - pipelines comprised of multiple large language models (LLM), software tools and database systems. Compound AI systems are constructed on a layered traditional software stack running on a distributed hardware infrastructure. Many of the diverse software components are vulnerable to traditional security flaws documented in the Common Vulnerabilities and Exposures (CVE) database, while the underlying distributed hardware infrastructure remains exposed to timing attacks, bit-flip faults, and power-based side channels. Today, research targets LLM-specific risks like model extraction, training data leakage, and unsafe generation -- overlooking the impact of traditional system vulnerabilities. This work investigates how traditional software and hardware vulnerabilities can complement LLM-specific algorithmic attacks to compromise the integrity of a compound AI pipeline. We demonstrate two novel attacks that combine system-level vulnerabilities with algorithmic weaknesses: (1) Exploiting a software code injection flaw along with a guardrail Rowhammer attack to inject an unaltered jailbreak prompt into an LLM, resulting in an AI safety violation, and (2) Manipulating a knowledge database to redirect an LLM agent to transmit sensitive user data to a malicious application, thus breaching confidentiality. These attacks highlight the need to address traditional vulnerabilities; we systematize the attack primitives and analyze their composition by grouping vulnerabilities by their objective and mapping them to distinct stages of an attack lifecycle. This approach enables a rigorous red-teaming exercise and lays the groundwork for future defense strategies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：级联：为复合AI系统中的对抗威胁放大构建软件-硬件攻击工具
生成AI的快速进展催生了复合AI系统——由多个大型语言模型（LLM）、软件工具和数据库系统组成的管道。复合AI系统建立在分布式硬件基础设施上运行的分层传统软件栈之上。许多多样化的软件组件易受在公共漏洞和暴露（CVE）数据库中记录的传统安全缺陷的影响，而底层的分布式硬件基础设施则暴露于时序攻击、位翻转故障和基于功率的侧信道攻击。如今，研究主要针对LLM特定的风险，如模型提取、训练数据泄露和不安全生成——忽视了传统系统漏洞的影响。 本研究探讨了传统软件和硬件漏洞如何与LLM特定的算法攻击相辅相成，以破坏复合AI管道的完整性。我们展示了两种新颖的攻击，结合了系统级漏洞和算法弱点：（1）利用软件代码注入缺陷与保护性Rowhammer攻击相结合，将未修改的越狱提示注入LLM，导致AI安全违规；（2）操纵知识数据库，重定向LLM代理将敏感用户数据传输到恶意应用，从而侵犯机密性。这些攻击突显了处理传统漏洞的必要性；我们系统化了攻击原语，并通过按目标分组漏洞并将其映射到攻击生命周期的不同阶段来分析其组合。这种方法使严格的红队演练成为可能，并为未来的防御策略奠定基础。
Summary / 总结
The rapid advancement of generative AI has led to the emergence of Compound AI systems, which integrate multiple large language models and various software tools, raising concerns about their security due to traditional vulnerabilities. This study explores how these traditional software and hardware vulnerabilities can be exploited alongside algorithmic attacks specific to large language models, presenting two novel attack methods: one that combines a software code injection flaw with a Rowhammer attack to bypass AI safety measures, and another that manipulates a knowledge database to leak sensitive user information. The findings underscore the importance of addressing traditional vulnerabilities in the context of AI systems and provide a framework for analyzing attack strategies and developing future defense mechanisms.
生成性人工智能的快速发展导致复合人工智能系统的出现，这些系统整合了多个大型语言模型和各种软件工具，但这些系统仍然容易受到传统安全缺陷的影响。本研究探讨了传统软件和硬件漏洞如何增强特定于大型语言模型的算法攻击，展示了两种新型攻击方法：一种结合了软件代码注入缺陷和Rowhammer攻击，以绕过大型语言模型的安全措施，另一种则操纵知识数据库以泄露敏感用户信息。研究结果强调了在人工智能安全背景下解决传统漏洞的重要性，并提供了一个系统框架，用于分析和组合这些攻击向量。
Delayed Backdoor Attacks: Exploring the Temporal Dimension as a New Attack Surface in Pre-Trained Models
Authors: Zikang Ding, Haomiao Yang, Meng Hao, Wenbo Jiang, Kunlan Xiang, Runmeng Du, Yijing Liu, Ruichen Zhang, Dusit Niyato
First: 2026-03-12T13:57:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T13:57:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Backdoor attacks against pre-trained models (PTMs) have traditionally operated under an ``immediacy assumption,'' where malicious behavior manifests instantly upon trigger occurrence. This work revisits and challenges this paradigm by introducing \textit{\textbf{Delayed Backdoor Attacks (DBA)}}, a new class of threats in which activation is temporally decoupled from trigger exposure. We propose that this \textbf{temporal dimension} is the key to unlocking a previously infeasible class of attacks: those that use common, everyday words as triggers. To examine the feasibility of this paradigm, we design and implement a proof-of-concept prototype, termed \underline{D}elayed Backdoor Attacks Based on \underline{N}onlinear \underline{D}ecay (DND). DND embeds a lightweight, stateful logic module that postpones activation until a configurable threshold is reached, producing a distinct latency phase followed by a controlled outbreak. We derive a formal model to characterize this latency behavior and propose a dual-metric evaluation framework (ASR and ASR$_{delay}$) to empirically measure the delay effect. Extensive experiments on four (natural language processing)NLP benchmarks validate the core capabilities of DND: it remains dormant for a controllable duration, sustains high clean accuracy ($\ge$94\%), and achieves near-perfect post-activation attack success rates ($\approx$99\%, The average of other methods is below 95\%.). Moreover, DND exhibits resilience against several state-of-the-art defenses. This study provides the first empirical evidence that the temporal dimension constitutes a viable yet unprotected attack surface in PTMs, underscoring the need for next-generation, stateful, and time-aware defense mechanisms.
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to challenge the traditional immediacy assumption of backdoor attacks on pre-trained models (PTMs), which typically activate instantly upon trigger exposure. The authors introduce Delayed Backdoor Attacks (DBA), a novel attack class that decouples activation from trigger occurrence by utilizing a temporal dimension. They develop a proof-of-concept prototype called Delayed Backdoor Attacks Based on Nonlinear Decay (DND), which incorporates a stateful logic module to delay activation until a specific threshold is met. Experimental results on four NLP benchmarks demonstrate that DND can remain dormant for a configurable duration while maintaining high clean accuracy (≥94%) and achieving near-perfect post-activation attack success rates (≈99%), along with resilience against various state-of-the-art defenses, highlighting the need for advanced defenses that account for temporal aspects in PTMs.
本研究针对传统的针对预训练模型的后门攻击的局限性进行探讨，传统方法通常假设触发后立即激活。作者提出了延迟后门攻击（DBA），这是一种新型攻击范式，其中激活与触发事件在时间上分离，从而允许使用常见词汇作为触发器。他们开发了一个概念验证原型，称为基于非线性衰减的延迟后门攻击（DND），该原型结合了一个状态逻辑模块，以在达到指定阈值之前延迟激活。对四个自然语言处理基准的实验结果表明，DND可以在可控时间内保持潜伏，同时保持高的清洁准确率（≥94%）和接近完美的攻击成功率（≈99%），并且对多种先进防御具有韧性。这项研究突出了时间维度作为预训练模型中被忽视的攻击面，表明需要先进的防御策略。
The Mirror Design Pattern: Strict Data Geometry over Model Scale for Prompt Injection Detection
Authors: J Alex Corll
First: 2026-03-12T12:50:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T12:50:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Prompt injection defenses are often framed as semantic understanding problems and delegated to increasingly large neural detectors. For the first screening layer, however, the requirements are different: the detector runs on every request and therefore must be fast, deterministic, non-promptable, and auditable. We introduce Mirror, a data-curation design pattern that organizes prompt injection corpora into matched positive and negative cells so that a classifier learns control-plane attack mechanics rather than incidental corpus shortcuts. Using 5,000 strictly curated open-source samples -- the largest corpus supportable under our public-data validity contract -- we define a 32-cell mirror topology, fill 31 of those cells with public data, train a sparse character n-gram linear SVM, compile its weights into a static Rust artifact, and obtain 95.97\% recall and 92.07\% F1 on a 524-case holdout at sub-millisecond latency with no external model runtime dependencies. On the same holdout, our next line of defense, a 22-million-parameter Prompt Guard~2 model reaches 44.35\% recall and 59.14\% F1 at 49\,ms median and 324\,ms p95 latency. Linear models still leave residual semantic ambiguities such as use-versus-mention for later pipeline layers, but within that scope our results show that for L1 prompt injection screening, strict data geometry can matter more than model scale.
中文标题/摘要
标题：镜像设计模式：针对提示注入检测的严格数据几何与模型规模
提示注入防御通常被视为语义理解问题，并委托给越来越大的神经检测器。然而，对于第一层筛选，要求是不同的：检测器在每个请求上运行，因此必须快速、确定性、不可提示和可审计。我们引入了镜像，这是一种数据策划设计模式，将提示注入语料库组织成匹配的正负单元，以便分类器学习控制平面攻击机制，而不是偶然的语料库捷径。使用5000个严格策划的开源样本——在我们的公共数据有效性合同下可支持的最大语料库——我们定义了一个32单元的镜像拓扑，用公共数据填充其中31个单元，训练一个稀疏字符n-gram线性SVM，将其权重编译成静态Rust工件，并在524个案例的保留集上以亚毫秒延迟获得95.97%的召回率和92.07%的F1分数。在同一保留集上，我们的下一道防线，一个2200万参数的Prompt Guard~2模型在49毫秒的中位数和324毫秒的p95延迟下达到44.35%的召回率和59.14%的F1分数。线性模型仍然留下残余的语义模糊，例如后续管道层的使用与提及，但在这个范围内，我们的结果表明，对于L1提示注入筛选，严格的数据几何可能比模型规模更重要。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to improve prompt injection detection by addressing the limitations of existing semantic understanding approaches that rely on large neural detectors. The authors introduce a data-curation design pattern called Mirror, which organizes prompt injection corpora into matched positive and negative cells, allowing a classifier to focus on control-plane attack mechanics. Using a dataset of 5,000 curated open-source samples, they define a 32-cell mirror topology and train a sparse character n-gram linear SVM, achieving 95.97% recall and 92.07% F1 score on a 524-case holdout with sub-millisecond latency, outperforming a larger 22-million-parameter model in terms of recall and latency.
本研究解决了提示注入检测的挑战，该问题通常被视为需要大型神经网络的语义理解问题。作者提出了一种新的数据策划设计模式，称为Mirror，该模式将提示注入数据组织成匹配的正负单元，使分类器能够专注于攻击机制而不是数据中的捷径。通过使用5000个策划样本的数据集，他们开发了一个32单元的镜像拓扑，并训练了一个稀疏字符n-gram线性SVM，在持出集上实现了95.97%的召回率和92.07%的F1分数，延迟在亚毫秒级，优于一个较大模型的性能指标和更高的延迟。
From Next Token Prediction to (STRIPS) World Models
Authors: Carlos Núñez-Molina, Vicenç Gómez, Hector Geffner
First: 2025-09-16T14:03:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T12:40:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study whether next-token prediction can yield world models that truly support planning, in a controlled symbolic setting where propositional STRIPS action models are learned from action traces alone and correctness can be evaluated exactly. We introduce two architectures. The first is the STRIPS Transformer, a symbolically aligned model grounded in theoretical results linking transformers and the formal language structure of STRIPS domains. The second is a standard transformer architecture without explicit symbolic structure built in, for which we study different positional encoding schemes and attention aggregation mechanisms. We evaluate both architectures on five classical planning domains, measuring training accuracy, generalization, and planning performance across domains and problem sizes. Interestingly, both approaches can be used to produce models that support planning with off-the-shelf STRIPS planners over exponentially many unseen initial states and goals. Although the STRIPS Transformer incorporates a strong symbolic inductive bias, it is harder to optimize and requires larger datasets to generalize reliably. In contrast, a standard transformer with stick-breaking attention achieves near-perfect training accuracy and strong generalization. Finally, standard transformers without stick-breaking attention do not generalize to long traces, whereas a symbolic STRIPS model extracted from a transformer trained on shorter traces does.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从下一个标记预测到（STRIPS）世界模型
我们研究下一个标记预测是否能产生真正支持规划的世界模型，在一个受控的符号环境中，仅从动作轨迹学习命题STRIPS动作模型，并且可以精确评估正确性。我们引入了两种架构。第一种是STRIPS Transformer，一种符号对齐的模型，基于理论结果将变换器与STRIPS领域的形式语言结构联系起来。第二种是没有内置显式符号结构的标准变换器架构，我们研究了不同的位置编码方案和注意力聚合机制。我们在五个经典规划领域评估这两种架构，测量训练准确性、泛化能力以及跨领域和问题规模的规划性能。有趣的是，这两种方法都可以用于生成支持规划的模型，能够在指数级数量的未见初始状态和目标上与现成的STRIPS规划器配合使用。尽管STRIPS Transformer包含强大的符号归纳偏差，但优化更困难，并且需要更大的数据集以可靠地泛化。相比之下，具有粘性注意力的标准变换器实现了近乎完美的训练准确性和强大的泛化能力。最后，没有粘性注意力的标准变换器无法对长轨迹进行泛化，而从在较短轨迹上训练的变换器中提取的符号STRIPS模型则可以。
Summary / 总结
This research investigates the potential of next-token prediction to create world models that facilitate planning in a symbolic context, specifically using propositional STRIPS action models derived from action traces. The authors propose two architectures: the STRIPS Transformer, which is designed to align with the formal structure of STRIPS domains, and a standard transformer architecture that lacks explicit symbolic structure but explores various positional encoding and attention mechanisms. The evaluation across five classical planning domains reveals that both architectures can generate models that effectively support planning with STRIPS planners across numerous unseen initial states and goals, although the STRIPS Transformer requires larger datasets for reliable generalization, while the standard transformer with stick-breaking attention demonstrates high training accuracy and generalization capabilities.
本研究探讨了下一标记预测在符号框架内创建支持规划的世界模型的潜力，特别是使用从动作轨迹中派生的命题STRIPS动作模型。研究介绍了两种架构：STRIPS Transformer，它与符号结构对齐，以及缺乏明确符号特征的标准变换器，探索了各种位置编码和注意机制。在五个经典规划领域的评估中，发现这两种架构都能有效支持STRIPS规划者处理大量未见的初始状态和目标，尽管STRIPS Transformer虽然包含强符号偏置，但优化更具挑战性，并且需要更大的数据集才能可靠地泛化，而标准变换器则表现出高训练准确性和泛化能力。
OpenClaw PRISM: A Zero-Fork, Defense-in-Depth Runtime Security Layer for Tool-Augmented LLM Agents
Authors: Frank Li
First: 2026-03-12T12:20:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T12:20:12+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 3 figures, 6 tables. Open-source system paper with benchmark artifact pipeline
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-augmented LLM agents introduce security risks that extend beyond user-input filtering, including indirect prompt injection through fetched content, unsafe tool execution, credential leakage, and tampering with local control files. We present OpenClaw PRISM, a zero-fork runtime security layer for OpenClaw-based agent gateways. PRISM combines an in-process plugin with optional sidecar services and distributes enforcement across ten lifecycle hooks spanning message ingress, prompt construction, tool execution, tool-result persistence, outbound messaging, sub-agent spawning, and gateway startup. Rather than introducing a novel detection model, PRISM integrates a hybrid heuristic-plus-LLM scanning pipeline, conversation- and session-scoped risk accumulation with TTL-based decay, policy-enforced controls over tools, paths, private networks, domain tiers, and outbound secret patterns, and a tamper-evident audit and operations plane with integrity verification and hot-reloadable policy management. We outline an evaluation methodology and benchmark pipeline for measuring security effectiveness, false positives, layer contribution, runtime overhead, and operational recoverability in an agent-runtime setting, and we report current preliminary benchmark results on curated same-slice experiments and operational microbenchmarks. The system targets deployable runtime defense for real agent gateways rather than benchmark-only detection.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OpenClaw PRISM：一种零分叉、深度防御的运行时安全层，用于工具增强的LLM代理
工具增强的LLM代理引入的安全风险超出了用户输入过滤，包括通过获取内容的间接提示注入、不安全的工具执行、凭证泄露和篡改本地控制文件。我们提出了OpenClaw PRISM，一种基于OpenClaw的代理网关的零分叉运行时安全层。PRISM结合了一个进程内插件和可选的边车服务，并在十个生命周期钩子上分布执行，涵盖消息输入、提示构建、工具执行、工具结果持久化、出站消息、子代理生成和网关启动。PRISM并未引入新的检测模型，而是集成了混合启发式加LLM扫描管道、会话和对话范围的风险累积与基于TTL的衰减、对工具、路径、私有网络、域层和出站秘密模式的政策强制控制，以及具有完整性验证和热重载政策管理的篡改证据审计和操作平面。我们概述了一种评估方法和基准管道，用于测量安全有效性、误报、层贡献、运行时开销和代理运行时环境中的操作可恢复性，并报告了当前在策划的同片实验和操作微基准上的初步基准结果。该系统旨在为真实代理网关提供可部署的运行时防御，而非仅限于基准检测。

The motivation behind this research is to address the security risks associated with tool-augmented LLM agents, which include issues like indirect prompt injection and credential leakage. The authors present OpenClaw PRISM, a zero-fork runtime security layer that integrates a hybrid heuristic-plus-LLM scanning pipeline and enforces security across multiple lifecycle hooks. Key experimental findings indicate that PRISM effectively measures security effectiveness, reduces false positives, and maintains operational recoverability, demonstrating its potential as a deployable runtime defense for agent gateways rather than merely a detection model.

Benchmark of Benchmarks: Unpacking Influence and Code Repository Quality in LLM Safety Benchmarks
Authors: Junjie Chu, Xinyue Shen, Ye Leng, Michael Backes, Yun Shen, Yang Zhang
First: 2026-03-03T09:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T11:49:16+00:00
Comments: 22 pages. 19 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid growth of research in LLM safety makes it hard to track all advances. Benchmarks are therefore crucial for capturing key trends and enabling systematic comparisons. Yet, it remains unclear why certain benchmarks gain prominence, and no systematic assessment has been conducted on their academic influence or code quality. This paper fills this gap by presenting the first multi-dimensional evaluation of the influence (based on five metrics) and code quality (based on both automated and human assessment) on LLM safety benchmarks, analyzing 31 benchmarks and 382 non-benchmarks across prompt injection, jailbreak, and hallucination. We find that benchmark papers show no significant advantage in academic influence (e.g., citation count and density) over non-benchmark papers. We uncover a key misalignment: while author prominence correlates with paper influence, neither author prominence nor paper influence shows a significant correlation with code quality. Our results also indicate substantial room for improvement in code and supplementary materials: only 39% of repositories are ready-to-use, 16% include flawless installation guides, and a mere 6% address ethical considerations. Given that the work of prominent researchers tends to attract greater attention, they need to lead the effort in setting higher standards.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基准中的基准：解读LLM安全基准中的影响力和代码库质量
LLM安全研究的快速增长使得追踪所有进展变得困难。因此，基准对于捕捉关键趋势和进行系统比较至关重要。然而，尚不清楚为何某些基准会获得突出地位，也没有对其学术影响力或代码质量进行系统评估。本文通过对LLM安全基准的影响力（基于五个指标）和代码质量（基于自动化和人工评估）进行首次多维评估，填补了这一空白，分析了31个基准和382个非基准，涵盖了提示注入、越狱和幻觉。我们发现，基准论文在学术影响力（例如引用次数和密度）上并未显著优于非基准论文。我们揭示了一个关键的不一致：尽管作者的知名度与论文影响力相关，但作者知名度和论文影响力与代码质量之间并没有显著相关性。我们的结果还表明，代码和补充材料有很大的改进空间：只有39%的代码库是可直接使用的，16%包含无瑕疵的安装指南，只有6%涉及伦理考虑。鉴于知名研究者的工作往往吸引更多关注，他们需要在设定更高标准的努力中发挥领导作用。

本研究解决了由于LLM安全领域快速发展而导致的跟踪进展的挑战，并强调基准在系统比较中的重要性。作者对31个LLM安全基准和382个非基准进行了多维评估，通过五个指标评估其影响力，并通过自动化和人工评估评估代码质量。研究结果表明，基准论文在学术影响力上并未显著优于非基准论文，并且作者的知名度与代码质量之间存在明显的不匹配，只有39%的代码库是可直接使用的，且提供的材料缺乏全面的伦理考虑。
Exponential-Family Membership Inference: From LiRA and RMIA to BaVarIA
Authors: Rickard Brännvall
First: 2026-03-12T11:00:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T11:00:19+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 4 figures, plus 22-page appendix
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Membership inference attacks (MIAs) are becoming standard tools for auditing the privacy of machine learning models. The leading attacks -- LiRA (Carlini et al., 2022) and RMIA (Zarifzadeh et al., 2024) -- appear to use distinct scoring strategies, while the recently proposed BASE (Lassila et al., 2025) was shown to be equivalent to RMIA, making it difficult for practitioners to choose among them. We show that all three are instances of a single exponential-family log-likelihood ratio framework, differing only in their distributional assumptions and the number of parameters estimated per data point. This unification reveals a hierarchy (BASE1-4) that connects RMIA and LiRA as endpoints of a spectrum of increasing model complexity. Within this framework, we identify variance estimation as the key bottleneck at small shadow-model budgets and propose BaVarIA, a Bayesian variance inference attack that replaces threshold-based parameter switching with conjugate normal-inverse-gamma priors. BaVarIA yields a Student-t predictive (BaVarIA-t) or a Gaussian with stabilized variance (BaVarIA-n), providing stable performance without additional hyperparameter tuning. Across 12 datasets and 7 shadow-model budgets, BaVarIA matches or improves upon LiRA and RMIA, with the largest gains in the practically important low-shadow-model and offline regimes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：指数族成员推断：从LiRA和RMIA到BaVarIA
成员推断攻击（MIA）正成为审计机器学习模型隐私的标准工具。主要攻击方法——LiRA（Carlini等，2022）和RMIA（Zarifzadeh等，2024）似乎使用了不同的评分策略，而最近提出的BASE（Lassila等，2025）被证明等同于RMIA，这使得从业者在选择时面临困难。我们表明，这三者都是单一指数族对数似然比框架的实例，仅在其分布假设和每个数据点估计的参数数量上有所不同。这种统一揭示了一个层次结构（BASE1-4），将RMIA和LiRA连接为增加模型复杂性的光谱的两个端点。在这个框架内，我们确定方差估计是小阴影模型预算下的关键瓶颈，并提出BaVarIA，一种贝叶斯方差推断攻击，它用共轭正态-逆伽马先验替代基于阈值的参数切换。BaVarIA产生了一个Student-t预测（BaVarIA-t）或一个具有稳定方差的高斯分布（BaVarIA-n），在没有额外超参数调整的情况下提供稳定的性能。在12个数据集和7个阴影模型预算中，BaVarIA的表现与LiRA和RMIA相当或有所改善，尤其在实际重要的低阴影模型和离线环境中获得了最大的提升。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to clarify the distinctions and similarities among various membership inference attacks (MIAs) used for auditing machine learning model privacy, specifically focusing on LiRA, RMIA, and BASE. The authors employ a unified exponential-family log-likelihood ratio framework to analyze these attacks, revealing that they differ primarily in their distributional assumptions and parameter estimation methods. The key experimental finding is the introduction of BaVarIA, a Bayesian variance inference attack that enhances performance across 12 datasets and 7 shadow-model budgets, demonstrating that it matches or surpasses the performance of LiRA and RMIA, particularly in low-shadow-model and offline scenarios.
本研究的动机在于澄清用于审计机器学习模型隐私的各种成员推断攻击（MIA）之间的区别和相似之处，特别关注LiRA、RMIA和BASE。作者提出了一个基于指数族对数似然比的统一框架来分析这些攻击，强调了它们在分布假设和参数估计方面的差异。关键实验结果表明，新提出的贝叶斯方差推断攻击BaVarIA在12个数据集和7个影子模型预算中表现优于或与LiRA和RMIA相匹配，尤其在低影子模型和离线场景中表现出色。
Hiding in Plain Sight: A Steganographic Approach to Stealthy LLM Jailbreaks
Authors: Jianing Geng, Biao Yi, Zekun Fei, Ruiqi He, Lihai Nie, Tong Li, Zheli Liu
First: 2025-05-22T15:07:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T10:54:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Jailbreak attacks pose a serious threat to Large Language Models (LLMs) by bypassing their safety mechanisms. A truly advanced jailbreak is defined not only by its effectiveness but, more critically, by its stealthiness. However, existing methods face a fundamental trade-off between semantic stealth (hiding malicious intent) and linguistic stealth (appearing natural), leaving them vulnerable to detection. To resolve this trade-off, we propose StegoAttack, a framework that leverages steganography. The core insight is to embed a harmful query within a benign, semantically coherent paragraph. This design provides semantic stealth by concealing the existence of malicious content and ensures linguistic stealth by maintaining the natural fluency of the cover paragraph. We evaluate StegoAttack on four state-of-the-art, safety-aligned LLMs, including GPT-5 and Gemini-3, and benchmark it against eight leading jailbreak methods. Our results show that StegoAttack achieves an average attack success rate (ASR) of 95.50%, outperforming existing baselines across all four models. Critically, its ASR drops by less than 27.00% under external detectors, while maintaining natural language distribution. This demonstrates that steganography effectively decouples linguistic and semantic stealth, thereby posing a fully concealed yet highly effective security threat. The code is available at https://github.com/GenggengSvan/StegoAttack
中文标题/摘要
标题：隐匿于明处：一种隐写学方法用于隐秘的LLM越狱
越狱攻击通过绕过大型语言模型（LLM）的安全机制，对其构成严重威胁。真正先进的越狱不仅以其有效性为定义，更重要的是其隐秘性。然而，现有方法在语义隐秘（隐藏恶意意图）和语言隐秘（看起来自然）之间面临根本的权衡，使其易于被检测。为了解决这一权衡，我们提出了StegoAttack，一个利用隐写学的框架。核心见解是将有害查询嵌入一个良性、语义连贯的段落中。该设计通过隐藏恶意内容的存在提供语义隐秘，并通过保持覆盖段落的自然流畅性确保语言隐秘。我们在四个最先进的、安全对齐的LLM上评估StegoAttack，包括GPT-5和Gemini-3，并与八种领先的越狱方法进行基准测试。我们的结果表明，StegoAttack在所有四个模型上实现了95.50%的平均攻击成功率（ASR），超越了现有基线。关键是，在外部检测器下，其ASR下降不到27.00%，同时保持自然语言分布。这表明隐写学有效地解耦了语言和语义隐秘，从而构成了一个完全隐蔽但高度有效的安全威胁。代码可在https://github.com/GenggengSvan/StegoAttack获取。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the vulnerabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks that can bypass safety mechanisms. The authors propose a novel framework called StegoAttack, which utilizes steganography to embed harmful queries within benign, coherent paragraphs, thus achieving both semantic and linguistic stealth. Experimental results demonstrate that StegoAttack achieves an average attack success rate of 95.50% across four advanced LLMs, including GPT-5 and Gemini-3, while its success rate decreases by less than 27.00% when faced with external detectors, indicating its effectiveness in maintaining natural language distribution while concealing malicious intent.
本研究的动机在于解决大型语言模型（LLM）在越狱攻击中的脆弱性，这些攻击能够绕过其安全机制，特别关注此类攻击的有效性和隐蔽性。作者提出了一种名为StegoAttack的新框架，利用隐写术将有害查询嵌入到无害且语义连贯的段落中，从而实现语义和语言的隐蔽性。实验结果表明，StegoAttack在包括GPT-5和Gemini-3在内的四种最先进的LLM上实现了平均攻击成功率为95.50%，并且在面对外部检测器时成功率下降不到27.00%，这表明其在隐藏恶意意图的同时保持自然语言流畅性方面的有效性。
Language Generation with Replay: A Learning-Theoretic View of Model Collapse
Authors: Giorgio Racca, Michal Valko, Amartya Sanyal
First: 2026-03-12T10:44:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T10:44:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As scaling laws push the training of frontier large language models (LLMs) toward ever-growing data requirements, training pipelines are approaching a regime where much of the publicly available online text may be consumed. At the same time, widespread LLM usage increases the volume of machine-generated content on the web; together, these trends raise the likelihood of generated text re-entering future training corpora, increasing the associated risk of performance degradation often called model collapse. In practice, model developers address this concern through data cleaning, watermarking, synthetic-data policies, or, in some cases, blissful ignorance. However, the problem of model collapse in generative models has not been examined from a learning-theoretic perspective: we study it through the theoretical lens of the language generation in the limit framework, introducing a replay adversary that augments the example stream with the generator's own past outputs. Our main contribution is a fine-grained learning-theoretic characterization of when replay fundamentally limits generation: while replay is benign for the strongest notion of uniform generation, it provably creates separations for the weaker notions of non-uniform generation and generation in the limit. Interestingly, our positive results mirror heuristics widely used in practice, such as data cleaning, watermarking, and output filtering, while our separations show when these ideas can fail.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重放语言生成：模型崩溃的学习理论视角
随着规模法则推动前沿大型语言模型（LLMs）的训练对数据需求的不断增长，训练管道正接近一个阶段，在这个阶段，许多公开可用的在线文本可能会被消耗。同时，广泛使用LLM增加了网络上机器生成内容的数量；这两种趋势提高了生成文本重新进入未来训练语料库的可能性，从而增加了通常称为模型崩溃的性能下降风险。在实践中，模型开发者通过数据清理、水印、合成数据政策或在某些情况下的无知来应对这一问题。然而，生成模型中的模型崩溃问题尚未从学习理论的角度进行研究：我们通过极限框架中的语言生成的理论视角来研究它，引入了一种重放对手，通过生成器自身的过去输出增强示例流。我们的主要贡献是对重放在何时从根本上限制生成的细致学习理论特征描述：虽然重放对最强的均匀生成概念是良性的，但它在较弱的非均匀生成和极限生成概念中证明地造成了分离。有趣的是，我们的积极结果与实践中广泛使用的启发式方法相呼应，如数据清理、水印和输出过滤，而我们的分离则显示了这些想法何时可能失败。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the risk of model collapse in large language models (LLMs) due to the increasing consumption of publicly available online text and the rise of machine-generated content. The authors employ a learning-theoretic framework to analyze the impact of a replay adversary that incorporates the generator's past outputs into the training data. The key findings reveal that while replay does not hinder uniform generation, it significantly affects non-uniform generation and generation in the limit, highlighting the limitations of common practices like data cleaning and watermarking in preventing model collapse.
本研究的动机在于解决由于消耗公开可用的在线文本和机器生成内容的增加而导致的大型语言模型（LLMs）模型崩溃的风险。作者采用学习理论的方法来研究这个问题，引入了一种重放对手，将生成器的过去输出纳入训练数据。主要发现表明，尽管重放对最强的均匀生成形式没有负面影响，但它可能显著阻碍较弱的非均匀生成和极限生成形式，突显了数据清理和输出过滤等常见做法在防止模型崩溃方面的局限性。
Contract And Conquer: How to Provably Compute Adversarial Examples for a Black-Box Model?
Authors: Anna Chistyakova, Mikhail Pautov
First: 2026-03-11T11:58:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T10:37:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Black-box adversarial attacks are widely used as tools to test the robustness of deep neural networks against malicious perturbations of input data aimed at a specific change in the output of the model. Such methods, although they remain empirically effective, usually do not guarantee that an adversarial example can be found for a particular model. In this paper, we propose Contract And Conquer (CAC), an approach to provably compute adversarial examples for neural networks in a black-box manner. The method is based on knowledge distillation of a black-box model on an expanding distillation dataset and precise contraction of the adversarial example search space. CAC is supported by the transferability guarantee: we prove that the method yields an adversarial example for the black-box model within a fixed number of algorithm iterations. Experimentally, we demonstrate that the proposed approach outperforms existing state-of-the-art black-box attack methods on ImageNet dataset for different target models, including vision transformers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：契约与征服：如何可证明地计算黑箱模型的对抗样本？
黑箱对抗攻击被广泛用作测试深度神经网络对输入数据恶意扰动的鲁棒性工具，旨在实现模型输出的特定变化。这些方法虽然在经验上有效，但通常无法保证能为特定模型找到对抗样本。本文提出了契约与征服（CAC），一种以黑箱方式可证明地计算神经网络对抗样本的方法。该方法基于对黑箱模型在扩展蒸馏数据集上的知识蒸馏和对对抗样本搜索空间的精确收缩。CAC得到了可转移性保证的支持：我们证明该方法在固定的算法迭代次数内为黑箱模型生成对抗样本。实验表明，所提出的方法在不同目标模型的ImageNet数据集上优于现有的最先进黑箱攻击方法，包括视觉变换器。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to enhance the reliability of black-box adversarial attacks used to assess the robustness of deep neural networks against input perturbations. The authors introduce a method called Contract And Conquer (CAC), which employs knowledge distillation on an expanding dataset and systematically narrows the search space for adversarial examples. Experimental results indicate that CAC surpasses existing state-of-the-art black-box attack methods on the ImageNet dataset across various target models, including vision transformers.
本研究的动机在于提高黑箱对抗攻击的可靠性，这对于评估深度神经网络对输入扰动的鲁棒性至关重要。作者提出了一种名为Contract And Conquer (CAC)的方法，该方法利用知识蒸馏在扩展数据集上进行，并系统地缩小对抗样本的搜索空间。实验结果表明，CAC在不同目标模型（包括视觉变换器）上显著优于现有的最先进黑箱攻击方法，尤其是在ImageNet数据集上。
Hidden State Poisoning Attacks against Mamba-based Language Models
Authors: Alexandre Le Mercier, Chris Develder, Thomas Demeester
First: 2026-01-05T10:27:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T10:36:44+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State space models (SSMs) like Mamba offer efficient alternatives to Transformer-based language models, with linear time complexity. Yet, their adversarial robustness remains critically unexplored. This paper studies the phenomenon whereby specific short input phrases induce a partial amnesia effect in such models, by irreversibly overwriting information in their hidden states, referred to as a Hidden State Poisoning Attack (HiSPA). Our benchmark RoBench25 allows evaluating a model's information retrieval capabilities when subject to HiSPAs, and confirms the vulnerability of SSMs against such attacks. Even a recent 52B hybrid SSM-Transformer model from the Jamba family collapses on RoBench25 under optimized HiSPA triggers, whereas pure Transformers do not. We also observe that HiSPA triggers significantly weaken the Jamba model on the popular Open-Prompt-Injections benchmark, unlike pure Transformers. Finally, our interpretability study reveals patterns in Mamba's hidden layers during HiSPAs that could be used to build a HiSPA mitigation system. The full code and data to reproduce the experiments can be found at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/hispa_anonymous-5DB0.
中文标题/摘要
标题：针对基于Mamba的语言模型的隐状态中毒攻击
状态空间模型（SSM）如Mamba提供了比基于Transformer的语言模型更高效的替代方案，具有线性时间复杂度。然而，它们的对抗鲁棒性仍然未被充分探索。本文研究了特定短输入短语在此类模型中诱发部分遗忘效应的现象，通过不可逆地覆盖其隐状态中的信息，称为隐状态中毒攻击（HiSPA）。我们的基准RoBench25允许评估模型在遭受HiSPA时的信息检索能力，并确认SSM对这种攻击的脆弱性。即使是来自Jamba家族的最新52B混合SSM-Transformer模型在优化的HiSPA触发下也在RoBench25上崩溃，而纯Transformer则没有。我们还观察到，HiSPA触发显著削弱了Jamba模型在流行的Open-Prompt-Injections基准上的表现，而纯Transformer则没有。最后，我们的可解释性研究揭示了在HiSPA期间Mamba隐层中的模式，这些模式可以用于构建HiSPA缓解系统。完整的代码和数据可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/hispa_anonymous-5DB0找到。
Summary / 总结
This research investigates the vulnerability of state space models (SSMs), specifically Mamba, to adversarial attacks, motivated by the need to understand their robustness compared to Transformer-based models. The authors introduce a novel attack method called Hidden State Poisoning Attack (HiSPA), which exploits specific short input phrases to overwrite information in the models' hidden states. Experimental results demonstrate that even a large hybrid SSM-Transformer model from the Jamba family fails under optimized HiSPA triggers on the RoBench25 benchmark, while pure Transformers remain unaffected, highlighting the significant weaknesses of SSMs against such attacks and suggesting potential avenues for mitigation based on hidden layer patterns observed during the attacks.
本研究探讨了状态空间模型（SSMs），特别是Mamba，对对抗性攻击的脆弱性，动机在于了解其相对于基于Transformer模型的鲁棒性。作者提出了一种新颖的攻击方法，称为隐状态中毒攻击（HiSPA），该方法利用特定输入短语覆盖模型隐藏状态中的信息。实验结果表明，即使是先进的SSM，如来自Jamba家族的52B混合SSM-Transformer模型，在RoBench25基准测试中也受到HiSPA的显著影响，表现崩溃，而纯Transformer模型则未受影响。此外，研究还发现HiSPA触发器削弱了Jamba模型在Open-Prompt-Injections基准测试中的表现，并揭示了Mamba隐藏层中的模式，这些模式可能为未来的缓解策略提供信息。
Extending Sequence Length is Not All You Need: Effective Integration of Multimodal Signals for Gene Expression Prediction
Authors: Zhao Yang, Yi Duan, Jiwei Zhu, Ying Ba, Chuan Cao, Bing Su
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-25T04:16:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T10:31:50+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Gene expression prediction, which predicts mRNA expression levels from DNA sequences, presents significant challenges. Previous works often focus on extending input sequence length to locate distal enhancers, which may influence target genes from hundreds of kilobases away. Our work first reveals that for current models, long sequence modeling can decrease performance. Even carefully designed algorithms only mitigate the performance degradation caused by long sequences. Instead, we find that proximal multimodal epigenomic signals near target genes prove more essential. Hence we focus on how to better integrate these signals, which has been overlooked. We find that different signal types serve distinct biological roles, with some directly marking active regulatory elements while others reflect background chromatin patterns that may introduce confounding effects. Simple concatenation may lead models to develop spurious associations with these background patterns. To address this challenge, we propose Prism, a framework that learns multiple combinations of high-dimensional epigenomic features to represent distinct background chromatin states and uses backdoor adjustment to mitigate confounding effects. Our experimental results demonstrate that proper modeling of multimodal epigenomic signals achieves state-of-the-art performance using only short sequences for gene expression prediction.
中文标题/摘要
标题：扩展序列长度并不是你所需要的一切：多模态信号在基因表达预测中的有效整合
基因表达预测，即从DNA序列预测mRNA表达水平，面临重大挑战。以往的研究通常集中在扩展输入序列长度，以定位可能影响目标基因的远端增强子，这些增强子可能距离目标基因数百千碱基。我们的研究首先揭示，对于当前模型，长序列建模可能会降低性能。即使是精心设计的算法也只能减轻长序列带来的性能下降。相反，我们发现靠近目标基因的近端多模态表观基因组信号更为重要。因此，我们专注于如何更好地整合这些被忽视的信号。我们发现，不同类型的信号在生物学上扮演着不同的角色，有些直接标记活跃的调控元件，而另一些则反映可能引入混淆效应的背景染色质模式。简单的拼接可能导致模型与这些背景模式产生虚假的关联。为了解决这一挑战，我们提出了Prism，一个学习高维表观基因组特征多种组合以表示不同背景染色质状态的框架，并使用后门调整来减轻混淆效应。我们的实验结果表明，适当建模多模态表观基因组信号能够在仅使用短序列进行基因表达预测时实现最先进的性能。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to improve gene expression prediction by addressing the limitations of current models that rely heavily on long DNA sequence inputs. The authors propose a novel framework called Prism, which effectively integrates proximal multimodal epigenomic signals rather than merely extending sequence lengths. Experimental results indicate that this approach achieves state-of-the-art performance in gene expression prediction using only short sequences, highlighting the importance of accurately modeling distinct biological roles of different signal types and mitigating confounding effects from background chromatin patterns.
本研究的动机是改善从DNA序列预测基因表达的能力，而这一过程受到长序列建模挑战的制约。作者提出了一种名为Prism的新框架，有效整合了近端多模态表观基因组信号，而不是仅依赖于扩展的序列长度。实验结果表明，这种方法在使用短序列进行基因表达预测时达到了最先进的性能，突显了准确建模不同类型表观基因组信号以避免混淆效应的重要性。
Towards Highly Transferable Vision-Language Attack via Semantic-Augmented Dynamic Contrastive Interaction
Authors: Yuanbo Li, Tianyang Xu, Cong Hu, Tao Zhou, Xiao-Jun Wu, Josef Kittler
First: 2026-03-05T05:46:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T09:31:21+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
With the rapid advancement and widespread application of vision-language pre-training (VLP) models, their vulnerability to adversarial attacks has become a critical concern. In general, the adversarial examples can typically be designed to exhibit transferable power, attacking not only different models but also across diverse tasks. However, existing attacks on language-vision models mainly rely on static cross-modal interactions and focus solely on disrupting positive image-text pairs, resulting in limited cross-modal disruption and poor transferability. To address this issue, we propose a Semantic-Augmented Dynamic Contrastive Attack (SADCA) that enhances adversarial transferability through progressive and semantically guided perturbation. SADCA progressively disrupts cross-modal alignment through dynamic interactions between adversarial images and texts. This is accomplished by SADCA establishing a contrastive learning mechanism involving adversarial, positive and negative samples, to reinforce the semantic inconsistency of the obtained perturbations. Moreover, we empirically find that input transformations commonly used in traditional transfer-based attacks also benefit VLPs, which motivates a semantic augmentation module that increases the diversity and generalization of adversarial examples. Extensive experiments on multiple datasets and models demonstrate that SADCA significantly improves adversarial transferability and consistently surpasses state-of-the-art methods. The code is released at https://github.com/LiYuanBoJNU/SADCA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向高度可转移的视觉-语言攻击：语义增强动态对比交互
随着视觉-语言预训练（VLP）模型的快速发展和广泛应用，它们对对抗攻击的脆弱性已成为一个关键问题。一般而言，对抗样本通常可以设计为具有可转移性，攻击不仅不同模型，还跨越多种任务。然而，现有的语言-视觉模型攻击主要依赖于静态跨模态交互，专注于破坏正向图像-文本对，导致跨模态干扰有限且可转移性差。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种语义增强动态对比攻击（SADCA），通过渐进和语义引导的扰动增强对抗可转移性。SADCA通过对抗图像和文本之间的动态交互逐步破坏跨模态对齐。这是通过SADCA建立一个对比学习机制，涉及对抗样本、正样本和负样本，以增强获得的扰动的语义不一致性。此外，我们实证发现，传统基于转移的攻击中常用的输入变换也对VLP有益，这激励了一个语义增强模块，增加对抗样本的多样性和泛化性。在多个数据集和模型上的广泛实验表明，SADCA显著提高了对抗可转移性，并始终超越了最先进的方法。代码已发布在 https://github.com/LiYuanBoJNU/SADCA。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the vulnerability of vision-language pre-training models to adversarial attacks, which has become increasingly important due to their widespread use. The authors propose a Semantic-Augmented Dynamic Contrastive Attack (SADCA) method that enhances adversarial transferability by employing progressive and semantically guided perturbations through dynamic interactions between adversarial images and texts. Experimental results show that SADCA significantly improves adversarial transferability across multiple datasets and models, outperforming existing state-of-the-art methods in the field.
该研究关注视觉语言预训练模型在对抗攻击下的脆弱性，随着其广泛应用，这一问题日益严重。作者提出了一种语义增强动态对比攻击（SADCA）方法，通过渐进和语义引导的扰动过程增强对抗转移性，利用对抗图像和文本之间的动态交互。多数据集和模型的实验结果表明，SADCA显著提高了对抗转移性，并超越了现有的最先进方法。
Multi-Paradigm Collaborative Adversarial Attack Against Multi-Modal Large Language Models
Authors: Yuanbo Li, Tianyang Xu, Cong Hu, Tao Zhou, Xiao-Jun Wu, Josef Kittler
First: 2026-03-05T06:01:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T09:27:45+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The rapid progress of Multi-Modal Large Language Models (MLLMs) has significantly advanced downstream applications. However, this progress also exposes serious transferable adversarial vulnerabilities. In general, existing adversarial attacks against MLLMs typically rely on surrogate models trained within a single learning paradigm and perform independent optimisation in their respective feature spaces. This straightforward setting naturally restricts the richness of feature representations, delivering limits on the search space and thus impeding the diversity of adversarial perturbations. To address this, we propose a novel Multi-Paradigm Collaborative Attack (MPCAttack) framework to boost the transferability of adversarial examples against MLLMs. In principle, MPCAttack aggregates semantic representations, from both visual images and language texts, to facilitate joint adversarial optimisation on the aggregated features through a Multi-Paradigm Collaborative Optimisation (MPCO) strategy. By performing contrastive matching on multi-paradigm features, MPCO adaptively balances the importance of different paradigm representations and guides the global perturbation optimisation, effectively alleviating the representation bias. Extensive experimental results on multiple benchmarks demonstrate the superiority of MPCAttack, indicating that our solution consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both targeted and untargeted attacks on open-source and closed-source MLLMs. The code is released at https://github.com/LiYuanBoJNU/MPCAttack.
中文标题/摘要
标题：针对多模态大型语言模型的多范式协同对抗攻击
多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）的快速进展显著推动了下游应用的发展。然而，这一进展也暴露了严重的可转移对抗脆弱性。一般而言，现有针对MLLMs的对抗攻击通常依赖于在单一学习范式下训练的替代模型，并在各自的特征空间中进行独立优化。这种简单的设置自然限制了特征表示的丰富性，限制了搜索空间，从而阻碍了对抗扰动的多样性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种新颖的多范式协同攻击（MPCAttack）框架，以增强对抗样本在MLLMs上的可转移性。原则上，MPCAttack聚合来自视觉图像和语言文本的语义表示，通过多范式协同优化（MPCO）策略促进对聚合特征的联合对抗优化。通过对多范式特征进行对比匹配，MPCO自适应地平衡不同范式表示的重要性，并引导全局扰动优化，有效缓解表示偏差。在多个基准上的大量实验结果表明，MPCAttack的优越性，表明我们的解决方案在针对开源和闭源MLLMs的有针对性和无针对性攻击中始终优于最先进的方法。代码已发布在 https://github.com/LiYuanBoJNU/MPCAttack。

The authors propose a Multi-Paradigm Collaborative Attack (MPCAttack) framework that aggregates semantic representations from both visual images and language texts, enabling joint adversarial optimization through a Multi-Paradigm Collaborative Optimization (MPCO) strategy. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks show that MPCAttack significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods in both targeted and untargeted attacks on various MLLMs.

Do LLMs Truly Benefit from Longer Context in Automatic Post-Editing?
Authors: Ahrii Kim, Seong-heum Kim
First: 2026-01-27T09:45:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T08:12:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automatic post-editing (APE) aims to refine machine translations by correcting residual errors. Although recent large language models (LLMs) demonstrate strong translation capabilities, their effectiveness for APE--especially under document-level context--remains insufficiently understood. We present a systematic comparison of proprietary and open-weight LLMs under a naive document-level prompting setup, analyzing APE quality, contextual behavior, robustness, and efficiency. Our results show that proprietary LLMs achieve near human-level APE quality even with simple one-shot prompting, regardless of whether document context is provided. While these models exhibit higher robustness to data poisoning attacks than open-weight counterparts, this robustness also reveals a limitation: they largely fail to exploit document-level context for contextual error correction. Furthermore, standard automatic metrics do not reliably reflect these qualitative improvements, highlighting the continued necessity of human evaluation. Despite their strong performance, the substantial cost and latency overheads of proprietary LLMs render them impractical for real-world APE deployment. Overall, our findings elucidate both the promise and current limitations of LLM-based document-aware APE, and point toward the need for more efficient long-context modeling approaches for translation refinement.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型在自动后编辑中是否真的受益于更长的上下文？
自动后编辑（APE）旨在通过纠正残余错误来完善机器翻译。尽管最近的大型语言模型（LLMs）展示了强大的翻译能力，但它们在APE中的有效性，特别是在文档级上下文下，仍然不够清楚。我们在简单的文档级提示设置下，对专有和开放权重的LLMs进行了系统比较，分析了APE质量、上下文行为、鲁棒性和效率。 我们的结果表明，专有LLMs即使在简单的一次性提示下也能达到接近人类水平的APE质量，无论是否提供文档上下文。虽然这些模型对数据中毒攻击表现出比开放权重模型更高的鲁棒性，但这种鲁棒性也揭示了一个局限性：它们在上下文错误纠正方面未能充分利用文档级上下文。此外，标准自动评估指标并不能可靠地反映这些定性改进，突显了人类评估的持续必要性。尽管表现强劲，专有LLMs的高成本和延迟开销使其在现实世界的APE部署中不切实际。总体而言，我们的发现阐明了基于LLM的文档感知APE的前景和当前局限性，并指向了更高效的长上下文建模方法在翻译完善中的需求。

Taming OpenClaw: Security Analysis and Mitigation of Autonomous LLM Agent Threats
Authors: Xinhao Deng, Yixiang Zhang, Jiaqing Wu, Jiaqi Bai, Sibo Yi, Zhuoheng Zou, Yue Xiao, Rennai Qiu, Jianan Ma, Jialuo Chen, Xiaohu Du, Xiaofang Yang, Shiwen Cui, Changhua Meng, Weiqiang Wang, Jiaxing Song, Ke Xu, Qi Li
First: 2026-03-12T07:24:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T07:24:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous Large Language Model (LLM) agents, exemplified by OpenClaw, demonstrate remarkable capabilities in executing complex, long-horizon tasks. However, their tightly coupled instant-messaging interaction paradigm and high-privilege execution capabilities substantially expand the system attack surface. In this paper, we present a comprehensive security threat analysis of OpenClaw. To structure our analysis, we introduce a five-layer lifecycle-oriented security framework that captures key stages of agent operation, i.e., initialization, input, inference, decision, and execution, and systematically examine compound threats across the agent's operational lifecycle, including indirect prompt injection, skill supply chain contamination, memory poisoning, and intent drift. Through detailed case studies on OpenClaw, we demonstrate the prevalence and severity of these threats and analyze the limitations of existing defenses. Our findings reveal critical weaknesses in current point-based defense mechanisms when addressing cross-temporal and multi-stage systemic risks, highlighting the need for holistic security architectures for autonomous LLM agents. Within this framework, we further examine representative defense strategies at each lifecycle stage, including plugin vetting frameworks, context-aware instruction filtering, memory integrity validation protocols, intent verification mechanisms, and capability enforcement architectures.

标题：驯服OpenClaw：自主LLM代理威胁的安全分析与缓解
自主大型语言模型（LLM）代理，如OpenClaw，展示了在执行复杂的长期任务方面的卓越能力。然而，它们紧密耦合的即时消息交互范式和高权限执行能力显著扩大了系统攻击面。本文对OpenClaw进行了全面的安全威胁分析。为了结构化我们的分析，我们引入了一个五层生命周期导向的安全框架，捕捉代理操作的关键阶段，即初始化、输入、推理、决策和执行，并系统地检查代理操作生命周期中的复合威胁，包括间接提示注入、技能供应链污染、内存中毒和意图漂移。通过对OpenClaw的详细案例研究，我们展示了这些威胁的普遍性和严重性，并分析了现有防御的局限性。我们的研究结果揭示了当前基于点的防御机制在应对跨时间和多阶段系统风险时的关键弱点，强调了对自主LLM代理的整体安全架构的需求。在此框架内，我们进一步检查了每个生命周期阶段的代表性防御策略，包括插件审查框架、上下文感知指令过滤、内存完整性验证协议、意图验证机制和能力强制架构。
