The Orthogonal Vulnerabilities of Generative AI Watermarks: A Comparative Empirical Benchmark of Spatial and Latent Provenance
Authors: Jesse Yu, Nicholas Wei
First: 2026-03-11T01:47:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T06:10:05+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As open-weights generative AI rapidly proliferates, the ability to synthesize hyper-realistic media has introduced profound challenges to digital trust. Automated disinformation and AI-generated imagery have made robust digital provenance a critical cybersecurity imperative. Currently, state-of-the-art invisible watermarks operate within one of two primary mathematical manifolds: the spatial domain (post-generation pixel embedding) or the latent domain (pre-generation frequency embedding). While existing literature frequently evaluates these models against isolated, classical distortions, there is a critical lack of rigorous, comparative benchmarking against modern generative AI editing tools. In this study, we empirically evaluate two leading representative paradigms, RivaGAN (Spatial) and Tree-Ring (Latent), utilizing an automated Attack Simulation Engine across 30 intensity intervals of geometric and generative perturbations. We formalize an "Adversarial Evasion Region" (AER) framework to measure cryptographic degradation against semantic visual retention (OpenCLIP > 75.0). Our statistical analysis ($n=100$ per interval, $MOE = \pm 3.92\%$) reveals that these domains possess mutually exclusive, mathematically orthogonal vulnerabilities. Spatial watermarks experience severe cryptographic degradation under algorithmic pixel-rewriting (exhibiting a 67.47% AER evasion rate under Img2Img translation), whereas latent watermarks exhibit profound fragility against geometric misalignment (yielding a 43.20% AER evasion rate under static cropping). By proving that single-domain watermarking is fundamentally insufficient against modern adversarial toolsets, this research exposes a systemic vulnerability in current digital provenance standards and establishes the foundational exigence for future multi-domain cryptographic architectures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：生成性人工智能水印的正交脆弱性：空间和潜在来源的比较实证基准
随着开放权重生成性人工智能的快速普及，合成超现实媒体的能力给数字信任带来了深刻挑战。自动化虚假信息和AI生成图像使得强大的数字来源成为网络安全的关键任务。目前，最先进的隐形水印在两种主要数学流形中运行：空间域（生成后像素嵌入）或潜在域（生成前频率嵌入）。尽管现有文献经常针对孤立的经典失真评估这些模型，但缺乏对现代生成性AI编辑工具的严格比较基准。在本研究中，我们通过自动化攻击模拟引擎在30个几何和生成扰动强度区间内实证评估了两个主要代表范式，RivaGAN（空间）和Tree-Ring（潜在）。我们正式化了一个“对抗逃避区域”（AER）框架，以测量针对语义视觉保留的密码学退化（OpenCLIP > 75.0）。我们的统计分析（每个区间$n=100$，$MOE = \pm 3.92\%$）揭示了这些领域具有相互排斥的数学正交脆弱性。空间水印在算法像素重写下经历严重的密码学退化（在Img2Img转换下表现出67.47%的AER逃避率），而潜在水印在几何失配下表现出深刻的脆弱性（在静态裁剪下产生43.20%的AER逃避率）。通过证明单域水印在现代对抗工具集面前根本不足，本研究揭示了当前数字来源标准的系统性脆弱性，并为未来多域密码学架构奠定了基础需求。

The findings indicate that spatial watermarks are highly susceptible to algorithmic pixel-rewriting, with a 67.47% evasion rate, while latent watermarks are particularly fragile to geometric misalignment, showing a 43.20% evasion rate, highlighting the need for multi-domain cryptographic architectures to address these vulnerabilities in digital provenance standards.

Deactivating Refusal Triggers: Understanding and Mitigating Overrefusal in Safety Alignment
Authors: Zhiyu Xue, Zimo Qi, Guangliang Liu, Bocheng Chen, Ramtin Pedarsani
First: 2026-03-12T00:07:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T00:07:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment aims to ensure that large language models (LLMs) refuse harmful requests by post-training on harmful queries paired with refusal answers. Although safety alignment is widely adopted in industry, the overrefusal problem where aligned LLMs also reject benign queries after safety alignment post-training, remains insufficiently studied. Such an issue degrades the usability of safety alignment in real-world applications. In this paper, we examine how overrefusal arises under safety alignment, and propose a mitigation strategy inspired by our findings. We define refusal triggers as linguistic cues in the training data that elicit refusal responses, safety alignment encourages LLMs to associate refusal triggers within a training sample with refusal responses, leading aligned LLMs to refuse harmful queries. However, the refusal triggers include not only harmful linguistic cues but also non-harmful cues, therefore causing overrefusal to benign queries. Building on this mechanistic analysis, we propose a method that explicitly considers refusal triggers in the safety alignment fine-tuning. Empirical results demonstrate that our approach achieves a more favorable trade-off between defense against jailbreak attacks and responsiveness to benign queries, outperforming prior methods. Warning: this paper contains harmful and biased sentences.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解除拒绝触发器：理解和缓解安全对齐中的过度拒绝
安全对齐旨在确保大型语言模型（LLMs）通过对有害查询进行后训练并配对拒绝答案来拒绝有害请求。尽管安全对齐在行业中被广泛采用，但过度拒绝问题，即对齐的LLMs在安全对齐后训练后也拒绝良性查询，仍然研究不足。这一问题降低了安全对齐在实际应用中的可用性。本文探讨了在安全对齐下过度拒绝是如何产生的，并提出了一种基于我们发现的缓解策略。我们将拒绝触发器定义为训练数据中的语言线索，这些线索引发拒绝响应，安全对齐鼓励LLMs将训练样本中的拒绝触发器与拒绝响应关联，从而导致对齐的LLMs拒绝有害查询。然而，拒绝触发器不仅包括有害语言线索，还包括无害线索，因此导致对良性查询的过度拒绝。在这一机制分析的基础上，我们提出了一种在安全对齐微调中明确考虑拒绝触发器的方法。实证结果表明，我们的方法在防御越狱攻击和对良性查询的响应之间实现了更有利的权衡，优于先前的方法。警告：本文包含有害和偏见的句子。

本研究的动机在于解决大型语言模型（LLMs）安全对齐中的过度拒绝问题，即这些模型在拒绝有害请求的同时也拒绝无害查询，从而影响可用性。作者研究了导致过度拒绝的机制，并提出了一种关注拒绝触发器的缓解策略——训练数据中促使拒绝响应的语言线索。实验结果表明，所提方法在防止有害请求和保持对无害查询的响应性之间取得了更好的平衡，优于现有方法。
Consistency of Large Reasoning Models Under Multi-Turn Attacks
Authors: Yubo Li, Ramayya Krishnan, Rema Padman
First: 2026-02-13T16:58:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T23:11:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large reasoning models with reasoning capabilities achieve state-of-the-art performance on complex tasks, but their robustness under multi-turn adversarial pressure remains underexplored. We evaluate nine frontier reasoning models under adversarial attacks. Our findings reveal that reasoning confers meaningful but incomplete robustness: most reasoning models studied significantly outperform instruction-tuned baselines, yet all exhibit distinct vulnerability profiles, with misleading suggestions universally effective and social pressure showing model-specific efficacy. Through trajectory analysis, we identify five failure modes (Self-Doubt, Social Conformity, Suggestion Hijacking, Emotional Susceptibility, and Reasoning Fatigue) with the first two accounting for 50% of failures. We further demonstrate that Confidence-Aware Response Generation (CARG), effective for standard LLMs, fails for reasoning models due to overconfidence induced by extended reasoning traces; counterintuitively, random confidence embedding outperforms targeted extraction. Our results highlight that reasoning capabilities do not automatically confer adversarial robustness and that confidence-based defenses require fundamental redesign for reasoning models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多轮攻击下大型推理模型的一致性
具有推理能力的大型推理模型在复杂任务上实现了最先进的性能，但它们在多轮对抗压力下的鲁棒性仍然未被充分探索。我们评估了九个前沿推理模型在对抗攻击下的表现。我们的研究发现，推理确实赋予了有意义但不完整的鲁棒性：大多数研究的推理模型显著优于指令调优基线，但所有模型都表现出不同的脆弱性特征，误导性建议普遍有效，而社会压力则显示出模型特定的有效性。通过轨迹分析，我们识别出五种失败模式（自我怀疑、社会从众、建议劫持、情感易感性和推理疲劳），前两种模式占据了50%的失败。我们进一步证明，信心感知响应生成（CARG）在标准LLM中有效，但由于延长推理轨迹引发的过度自信，在推理模型中失效；反直觉的是，随机信心嵌入的表现优于针对性提取。我们的结果强调，推理能力并不自动赋予对抗鲁棒性，基于信心的防御需要对推理模型进行根本性重新设计。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates the robustness of large reasoning models under multi-turn adversarial attacks, motivated by their state-of-the-art performance on complex tasks yet unexplored vulnerability. The study evaluates nine advanced reasoning models against various adversarial strategies, revealing that while these models outperform instruction-tuned baselines, they exhibit distinct vulnerabilities, particularly to misleading suggestions and social pressure. Through trajectory analysis, five failure modes are identified, with Self-Doubt and Social Conformity accounting for half of the failures, and it is shown that existing confidence-based defenses like Confidence-Aware Response Generation (CARG) are ineffective for reasoning models due to induced overconfidence, suggesting that new defense strategies are necessary.
本研究探讨了大型推理模型在多轮对抗攻击下的鲁棒性，动机在于这些模型在复杂任务上表现出色，但其脆弱性尚未得到充分理解。研究评估了九种先进的推理模型在各种对抗策略下的表现，结果显示，尽管这些模型的表现优于基于指令的基线，但它们在误导性建议和社会压力等方面表现出明显的脆弱性。通过轨迹分析，识别出五种失败模式，其中自我怀疑和社会从众占据了一半的失败案例，并且研究表明，现有的基于信心的防御措施如信心感知响应生成在推理模型中效果不佳，需重新设计此类防御以提高鲁棒性。
MirrorDrift: Actuated Mirror-Based Attacks on LiDAR SLAM
Authors: Rokuto Nagata, Kenji Koide, Kazuma Ikeda, Ozora Sako, Shion Horie, Kentaro Yoshioka
First: 2026-03-11T23:03:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T23:03:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LiDAR SLAM provides high-accuracy localization but is fragile to point-cloud corruption because scan matching assumes geometric consistency. Prior physical attacks on LiDAR SLAM largely rely on LiDAR spoofing via external signal injection, which requires sensor-specific timing knowledge and is increasingly mitigated by modern defense mechanisms such as timing obfuscation and injection rejection. In this work, we show that specular reflection offers an injection-free alternative and demonstrate an attack, MirrorDrift, that uses an actuated planar mirror to cause ghost points in LiDAR scans and systematically bias scan-matching correspondences. MirrorDrift optimizes mirror placement, alignment, and actuation. In simulation, it increases the average pose error (APE) by 6.1x over random placement, degrading three SLAM systems to 2.29-3.31 m mean APE. In real-world experiments on a modern LiDAR with state-of-the-art interference mitigation, it induces localization errors of up to 6.03 m. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first successful SLAM-targeted attack against production-grade secure LiDARs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MirrorDrift：基于驱动镜的LiDAR SLAM攻击
LiDAR SLAM提供高精度定位，但对点云损坏非常脆弱，因为扫描匹配假设几何一致性。之前对LiDAR SLAM的物理攻击主要依赖于通过外部信号注入进行的LiDAR欺骗，这需要传感器特定的时序知识，并且越来越多地被现代防御机制（如时序混淆和注入拒绝）所缓解。在这项工作中，我们展示了镜面反射提供了一种无注入的替代方案，并演示了一种攻击，MirrorDrift，利用驱动平面镜在LiDAR扫描中造成虚假点，并系统性地偏置扫描匹配对应关系。MirrorDrift优化了镜子的放置、对齐和驱动。在仿真中，它使平均姿态误差（APE）比随机放置增加6.1倍，使三个SLAM系统的平均APE降至2.29-3.31米。在现代LiDAR的真实世界实验中，尽管采用了最先进的干扰缓解技术，它仍然导致高达6.03米的定位误差。据我们所知，这是针对生产级安全LiDAR的首次成功SLAM目标攻击。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the vulnerabilities of LiDAR SLAM systems to point-cloud corruption, particularly in light of modern defense mechanisms against traditional spoofing attacks. The authors introduce a novel attack method called MirrorDrift, which utilizes an actuated planar mirror to create ghost points in LiDAR scans, thereby biasing scan-matching correspondences without the need for signal injection. Experimental results show that in simulations, MirrorDrift increases the average pose error by 6.1 times compared to random mirror placement, resulting in mean pose errors of 2.29-3.31 meters across three SLAM systems, while real-world tests on a modern LiDAR system demonstrate localization errors of up to 6.03 meters, marking it as the first successful attack on secure LiDARs designed for SLAM applications.
本研究的动机在于解决LiDAR SLAM系统的脆弱性，这些系统由于依赖几何一致性而容易受到点云损坏的影响。作者提出了一种新颖的攻击方法，称为MirrorDrift，该方法利用一个可动平面镜子在LiDAR扫描中创建虚假点，而无需信号注入。实验结果表明，在模拟中，MirrorDrift相比随机镜子放置增加了6.1倍的平均姿态误差，使得三个SLAM系统的平均姿态误差达到2.29-3.31米。在现实世界的测试中，该攻击导致的定位误差高达6.03米，这标志着这是对设计用于SLAM应用的安全LiDAR系统的首次成功攻击。
Jailbreak Scaling Laws for Large Language Models: Polynomial-Exponential Crossover
Authors: Indranil Halder, Annesya Banerjee, Cengiz Pehlevan
First: 2026-03-11T21:48:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T21:48:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Adversarial attacks can reliably steer safety-aligned large language models toward unsafe behavior. Empirically, we find that adversarial prompt-injection attacks can amplify attack success rate from the slow polynomial growth observed without injection to exponential growth with the number of inference-time samples. To explain this phenomenon, we propose a theoretical generative model of proxy language in terms of a spin-glass system operating in a replica-symmetry-breaking regime, where generations are drawn from the associated Gibbs measure and a subset of low-energy, size-biased clusters is designated unsafe. Within this framework, we analyze prompt injection-based jailbreaking. Short injected prompts correspond to a weak magnetic field aligned towards unsafe cluster centers and yield a power-law scaling of attack success rate with the number of inference-time samples, while long injected prompts, i.e., strong magnetic field, yield exponential scaling. We derive these behaviors analytically and confirm them empirically on large language models. This transition between two regimes is due to the appearance of an ordered phase in the spin chain under a strong magnetic field, which suggests that the injected jailbreak prompt enhances adversarial order in the language model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型的越狱扩展法则：多项式-指数交叉
对抗性攻击可以可靠地引导安全对齐的大型语言模型朝向不安全行为。实证研究发现，对抗性提示注入攻击可以将攻击成功率从没有注入时观察到的缓慢多项式增长放大到与推理时间样本数量相关的指数增长。为了解释这一现象，我们提出了一个理论生成模型，描述了在复制对称破缺状态下运行的代理语言的自旋玻璃系统，其中生成是从相关的吉布斯测度中抽取的，并且一部分低能量、大小偏向的簇被指定为不安全。在这个框架内，我们分析了基于提示注入的越狱。短的注入提示对应于朝向不安全簇中心对齐的弱磁场，并且随着推理时间样本数量的增加，攻击成功率呈幂律扩展，而长的注入提示，即强磁场，则呈指数扩展。我们从理论上推导了这些行为，并在大型语言模型上进行了实证验证。这两种状态之间的转变是由于在强磁场下自旋链中出现有序相，这表明注入的越狱提示增强了语言模型中的对抗性秩序。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates the vulnerability of safety-aligned large language models to adversarial attacks, specifically focusing on how prompt-injection can influence their behavior. The authors develop a theoretical generative model based on a spin-glass system to explain the observed phenomena, analyzing the scaling of attack success rates with varying lengths of injected prompts. They find that short prompts lead to polynomial growth in attack success rates, while longer prompts result in exponential growth, confirming these findings through empirical tests on large language models.
本研究探讨了对抗性攻击如何使安全对齐的大型语言模型表现出不安全行为，动机在于理解和减轻这些脆弱性。作者提出了一种基于自旋玻璃系统的理论生成模型，以解释攻击成功率随着推理时间样本增加而从多项式增长转变为指数增长的现象。实验结果表明，短促注入导致成功率呈幂律增长，而较长的促注入则导致指数增长，验证了理论预测，并突出了注入促在增强模型中的对抗性秩序方面的作用。
Systematic Scaling Analysis of Jailbreak Attacks in Large Language Models
Authors: Xiangwen Wang, Ananth Balashankar, Varun Chandrasekaran
First: 2026-03-11T17:38:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T17:38:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models remain vulnerable to jailbreak attacks, yet we still lack a systematic understanding of how jailbreak success scales with attacker effort across methods, model families, and harm types. We initiate a scaling-law framework for jailbreaks by treating each attack as a compute-bounded optimization procedure and measuring progress on a shared FLOPs axis. Our systematic evaluation spans four representative jailbreak paradigms, covering optimization-based attacks, self-refinement prompting, sampling-based selection, and genetic optimization, across multiple model families and scales on a diverse set of harmful goals. We investigate scaling laws that relate attacker budget to attack success score by fitting a simple saturating exponential function to FLOPs--success trajectories, and we derive comparable efficiency summaries from the fitted curves. Empirically, prompting-based paradigms tend to be the most compute-efficient compared to optimization-based methods. To explain this gap, we cast prompt-based updates into an optimization view and show via a same-state comparison that prompt-based attacks more effectively optimize in prompt space. We also show that attacks occupy distinct success--stealthiness operating points with prompting-based methods occupying the high-success, high-stealth region. Finally, we find that vulnerability is strongly goal-dependent: harms involving misinformation are typically easier to elicit than other non-misinformation harms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型越狱攻击的系统化规模分析
大型语言模型仍然容易受到越狱攻击，但我们仍然缺乏对越狱成功如何随着攻击者努力在方法、模型家族和伤害类型之间扩展的系统理解。我们通过将每次攻击视为一个计算受限的优化过程，并在共享的FLOPs轴上测量进展，启动了一个越狱的规模法则框架。我们的系统评估涵盖了四种代表性的越狱范式，包括基于优化的攻击、自我优化提示、基于采样的选择和遗传优化，跨越多个模型家族和规模，针对多种有害目标。我们通过将简单的饱和指数函数拟合到FLOPs-成功轨迹，研究了攻击者预算与攻击成功分数之间的规模法则，并从拟合曲线中得出可比的效率总结。从经验上看，与基于优化的方法相比，基于提示的范式往往是计算效率最高的。为了说明这一差距，我们将基于提示的更新视为一种优化视角，并通过同态比较显示基于提示的攻击在提示空间中更有效地进行优化。我们还表明，攻击在成功-隐蔽性操作点上占据不同的位置，基于提示的方法占据高成功、高隐蔽性的区域。最后，我们发现脆弱性与目标密切相关：涉及错误信息的伤害通常比其他非错误信息的伤害更容易引发。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to systematically understand the scaling of jailbreak attacks in large language models, which remain susceptible to such vulnerabilities. The authors employ a scaling-law framework that treats each attack as a compute-bounded optimization procedure, measuring progress along a shared FLOPs axis across various attack methods and model families. The key findings indicate that prompting-based paradigms are more compute-efficient than optimization-based methods, with distinct success-stealthiness operating points, and that the ease of eliciting harm is significantly influenced by the type of goal, particularly showing that misinformation harms are generally easier to achieve.
本研究的动机在于系统地理解大型语言模型中的越狱攻击的规模化，尽管存在多种方法，这些模型仍然脆弱。作者采用规模法框架，将每次攻击视为计算受限的优化过程，并在共享的FLOPs轴上测量进展，涵盖四种越狱范式。主要发现表明，与基于优化的方法相比，基于提示的范式在计算效率上更高，基于提示的攻击在提示空间中更有效地优化，并实现了更高的成功率和隐蔽性。此外，研究还揭示了模型的脆弱性高度依赖于伤害类型，涉及错误信息的攻击通常比其他形式的伤害更容易执行。
Cluster-Aware Attacks on Graph Watermarks
Authors: Alexander Nemecek, Emre Yilmaz, Erman Ayday
First: 2025-04-24T22:49:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T16:39:19+00:00
Comments: 20 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graph-structured datasets are increasingly central to sensitive applications spanning social networks, biomedical research, and cryptographic systems. As organizations share these datasets with trusted parties for collaborative analysis, protecting against unauthorized redistribution becomes critical. Graph watermarking addresses this challenge by embedding detectable signatures that enable ownership verification and attribution of leaked data. However, despite advances in watermarking techniques, existing robustness evaluations remain limited to random edge perturbation attacks, overlooking more sophisticated adversaries who exploit community structure present in real-world graphs. We introduce the first systematic evaluation of cluster-aware attacks on graph watermarking schemes. We present a threat model in which adversaries leverage community detection algorithms to guide strategic edge modifications, targeting either intra-cluster densification with inter-cluster boundary removal, or intra-cluster sparsification with inter-cluster noise injection. Evaluating against the most comprehensively tested watermarking scheme, we demonstrate that cluster-aware attacks outperform random perturbations across real-world datasets and clustering algorithms. Our findings reveal that cluster-aware attacks reduce attribution accuracy while introducing comparable structural distortion to random attacks, demonstrating superior attack efficiency. These results establish that current watermarking schemes, evaluated solely against random perturbations, remain vulnerable to structure-aware adversarial behavior, highlighting the need for robust defenses that account for community-exploiting adversaries in graph-based privacy protection systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于聚类的图水印攻击
图结构数据集在社交网络、生物医学研究和密码系统等敏感应用中越来越重要。随着组织与可信方共享这些数据集以进行协作分析，防止未经授权的再分发变得至关重要。图水印技术通过嵌入可检测的签名来解决这一挑战，从而实现所有权验证和泄露数据的归属。然而，尽管水印技术有所进展，现有的鲁棒性评估仍然局限于随机边扰动攻击，忽视了利用真实世界图中社区结构的更复杂对手。我们首次系统性地评估了针对图水印方案的基于聚类的攻击。我们提出了一种威胁模型，其中对手利用社区检测算法指导战略性边修改，目标是通过去除跨聚类边界实现聚类内密集化，或通过注入跨聚类噪声实现聚类内稀疏化。针对经过全面测试的水印方案进行评估，我们证明基于聚类的攻击在真实世界数据集和聚类算法中优于随机扰动。我们的研究结果表明，基于聚类的攻击降低了归属准确性，同时引入了与随机攻击相当的结构扭曲，显示出更高的攻击效率。这些结果表明，当前仅针对随机扰动进行评估的水印方案仍然容易受到结构感知对手行为的攻击，强调了在基于图的隐私保护系统中需要考虑利用社区的对手的鲁棒防御。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this research stems from the increasing importance of graph-structured datasets in sensitive applications and the need to protect these datasets from unauthorized redistribution. The authors introduce a systematic evaluation of cluster-aware attacks on graph watermarking schemes, employing a threat model where adversaries use community detection algorithms to strategically modify edges. The experimental results show that these cluster-aware attacks significantly outperform random perturbations in terms of reducing attribution accuracy while maintaining similar structural distortion, indicating that existing watermarking techniques are vulnerable to more sophisticated adversarial strategies that exploit community structures in graphs.
本研究的动机是图结构数据集在敏感应用中的重要性日益增加，以及保护这些数据集免受未经授权重新分发的需求。作者引入了对图水印方案的集群感知攻击的系统评估，攻击者利用社区检测算法来战略性地修改边。实验结果表明，这些集群感知攻击在降低归属准确性方面显著优于随机扰动，同时保持相似的结构扭曲水平，表明当前的水印技术对利用图中社区结构的更复杂的对抗策略存在脆弱性。
